5057 void MacroAssembler::reinit_heapbase() {
5058   if (UseCompressedOops || UseCompressedClassPointers) {
5059     if (Universe::heap() != NULL) {
5060       if (CompressedOops::base() == NULL) {
5061         MacroAssembler::xorptr(r12_heapbase, r12_heapbase);
5062       } else {
5063         mov64(r12_heapbase, (int64_t)CompressedOops::ptrs_base());
5064       }
5065     } else {
5066       movptr(r12_heapbase, ExternalAddress((address)CompressedOops::ptrs_base_addr()));
5067     }
5068   }
5069 }
5070 
5071 #endif // _LP64
5072 
5073 // C2 compiled method's prolog code.
5074 void MacroAssembler::verified_entry(Compile* C, int sp_inc) {
5075   int framesize = C->output()->frame_size_in_bytes();
5076   int bangsize = C->output()->bang_size_in_bytes();
5077   bool fp_mode_24b = false;
5078   int stack_bang_size = C->output()->need_stack_bang(bangsize) ? bangsize : 0;
5079 
5080   // WARNING: Initial instruction MUST be 5 bytes or longer so that
5081   // NativeJump::patch_verified_entry will be able to patch out the entry
5082   // code safely. The push to verify stack depth is ok at 5 bytes,
5083   // the frame allocation can be either 3 or 6 bytes. So if we don't do
5084   // stack bang then we must use the 6 byte frame allocation even if
5085   // we have no frame. :-(
5086   assert(stack_bang_size >= framesize || stack_bang_size <= 0, "stack bang size incorrect");
5087 
5088   assert((framesize & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "frame size not aligned");
5089   // Remove word for return addr
5090   framesize -= wordSize;
5091   stack_bang_size -= wordSize;
5092 
5093   // Calls to C2R adapters often do not accept exceptional returns.
5094   // We require that their callers must bang for them.  But be careful, because
5095   // some VM calls (such as call site linkage) can use several kilobytes of
5096   // stack.  But the stack safety zone should account for that.
5097   // See bugs 4446381, 4468289, 4497237.
5098   if (stack_bang_size > 0) {
5099     generate_stack_overflow_check(stack_bang_size);
5100 
5101     // We always push rbp, so that on return to interpreter rbp, will be
5102     // restored correctly and we can correct the stack.
5103     push(rbp);
5104     // Save caller's stack pointer into RBP if the frame pointer is preserved.
5105     if (PreserveFramePointer) {
5106       mov(rbp, rsp);
5107     }
5108     // Remove word for ebp
5109     framesize -= wordSize;
5110 
5111     // Create frame
5112     if (framesize) {
5113       subptr(rsp, framesize);
5114     }
5115   } else {
5116     // Create frame (force generation of a 4 byte immediate value)
5117     subptr_imm32(rsp, framesize);
5118 
5119     // Save RBP register now.
5120     framesize -= wordSize;
5121     movptr(Address(rsp, framesize), rbp);
5122     // Save caller's stack pointer into RBP if the frame pointer is preserved.
5123     if (PreserveFramePointer) {
5124       movptr(rbp, rsp);
5125       if (framesize > 0) {
5126         addptr(rbp, framesize);
5127       }
5128     }
5129   }
5130 
5131   if (C->needs_stack_repair()) {
5132     // Save stack increment (also account for fixed framesize and rbp)
5133     assert((sp_inc & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "stack increment not aligned");
5134     movptr(Address(rsp, C->output()->sp_inc_offset()), sp_inc + framesize + wordSize);
5135   }
5136 
5137   if (VerifyStackAtCalls) { // Majik cookie to verify stack depth
5138     framesize -= wordSize;
5139     movptr(Address(rsp, framesize), (int32_t)0xbadb100d);
5140   }
5141 
5142 #ifndef _LP64
5143   // If method sets FPU control word do it now
5144   if (fp_mode_24b) {
5145     fldcw(ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::addr_fpu_cntrl_wrd_24()));
5146   }
5147   if (UseSSE >= 2 && VerifyFPU) {
5148     verify_FPU(0, "FPU stack must be clean on entry");
5149   }
5150 #endif
5151 
5152 #ifdef ASSERT
5153   if (VerifyStackAtCalls) {
5154     Label L;
5155     push(rax);
5156     mov(rax, rsp);
5157     andptr(rax, StackAlignmentInBytes-1);
5158     cmpptr(rax, StackAlignmentInBytes-wordSize);
5159     pop(rax);
5160     jcc(Assembler::equal, L);
5161     STOP("Stack is not properly aligned!");
5162     bind(L);
5163   }
5164 #endif
5165 }
5166 
5167 // clear memory of size 'cnt' qwords, starting at 'base' using XMM/YMM registers
5168 void MacroAssembler::xmm_clear_mem(Register base, Register cnt, Register val, XMMRegister xtmp) {
5169   // cnt - number of qwords (8-byte words).
5170   // base - start address, qword aligned.
5171   Label L_zero_64_bytes, L_loop, L_sloop, L_tail, L_end;
5172   movdq(xtmp, val);
5173   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5174     punpcklqdq(xtmp, xtmp);
5175     vinserti128_high(xtmp, xtmp);
5176   } else {
5177     punpcklqdq(xtmp, xtmp);
5178   }
5179   jmp(L_zero_64_bytes);
5180 
5181   BIND(L_loop);
5182   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5183     vmovdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5184     vmovdqu(Address(base, 32), xtmp);
5185   } else {
5186     movdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5187     movdqu(Address(base, 16), xtmp);
5188     movdqu(Address(base, 32), xtmp);
5189     movdqu(Address(base, 48), xtmp);
5190   }
5191   addptr(base, 64);
5192 
5193   BIND(L_zero_64_bytes);
5194   subptr(cnt, 8);
5195   jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_loop);
5196   addptr(cnt, 4);
5197   jccb(Assembler::less, L_tail);
5198   // Copy trailing 32 bytes
5199   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5200     vmovdqu(Address(base, 0), xtmp);
5201   } else {
5202     movdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5203     movdqu(Address(base, 16), xtmp);
5204   }
5205   addptr(base, 32);
5206   subptr(cnt, 4);
5207 
5208   BIND(L_tail);
5209   addptr(cnt, 4);
5210   jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_end);
5211   decrement(cnt);
5212 
5213   BIND(L_sloop);
5214   movq(Address(base, 0), xtmp);
5215   addptr(base, 8);
5216   decrement(cnt);
5217   jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_sloop);
5218   BIND(L_end);
5219 }
5220 
5221 int MacroAssembler::store_value_type_fields_to_buf(ciValueKlass* vk, bool from_interpreter) {
5222   // A value type might be returned. If fields are in registers we
5223   // need to allocate a value type instance and initialize it with
5224   // the value of the fields.
5225   Label skip;
5226   // We only need a new buffered value if a new one is not returned
5227   testptr(rax, 1);
5228   jcc(Assembler::zero, skip);
5229   int call_offset = -1;
5230 
5231 #ifdef _LP64
5232   Label slow_case;
5233 
5234   // Try to allocate a new buffered value (from the heap)
5235   if (UseTLAB) {
5236     // FIXME -- for smaller code, the inline allocation (and the slow case) should be moved inside the pack handler.
5237     if (vk != NULL) {
5238       // Called from C1, where the return type is statically known.
5239       movptr(rbx, (intptr_t)vk->get_ValueKlass());
5240       jint lh = vk->layout_helper();
5241       assert(lh != Klass::_lh_neutral_value, "inline class in return type must have been resolved");
5242       movl(r14, lh);
5243     } else {
5244       // Call from interpreter. RAX contains ((the ValueKlass* of the return type) | 0x01)
5245       mov(rbx, rax);
5246       andptr(rbx, -2);
5247       movl(r14, Address(rbx, Klass::layout_helper_offset()));
5248     }
5249 
5250     movptr(r13, Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())));
5251     lea(r14, Address(r13, r14, Address::times_1));
5252     cmpptr(r14, Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_end_offset())));
5253     jcc(Assembler::above, slow_case);
5254     movptr(Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())), r14);
5255     movptr(Address(r13, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes()), (intptr_t)markWord::always_locked_prototype().value());
5256 
5257     xorl(rax, rax); // use zero reg to clear memory (shorter code)
5258     store_klass_gap(r13, rax);  // zero klass gap for compressed oops
5259 
5260     if (vk == NULL) {
5261       // store_klass corrupts rbx, so save it in rax for later use (interpreter case only).
5262       mov(rax, rbx);
5263     }
5264     store_klass(r13, rbx);  // klass
5265 
5266     // We have our new buffered value, initialize its fields with a
5267     // value class specific handler
5268     if (vk != NULL) {
5269       // FIXME -- do the packing in-line to avoid the runtime call
5270       mov(rax, r13);
5271       call(RuntimeAddress(vk->pack_handler())); // no need for call info as this will not safepoint.
5272     } else {
5273       movptr(rbx, Address(rax, InstanceKlass::adr_valueklass_fixed_block_offset()));
5274       movptr(rbx, Address(rbx, ValueKlass::pack_handler_offset()));
5275       mov(rax, r13);
5276       call(rbx);
5277     }
5278     jmp(skip);
5279   }
5280 
5281   bind(slow_case);
5282   // We failed to allocate a new value, fall back to a runtime
5283   // call. Some oop field may be live in some registers but we can't
5284   // tell. That runtime call will take care of preserving them
5285   // across a GC if there's one.
5286 #endif
5287 
5288   if (from_interpreter) {
5289     super_call_VM_leaf(StubRoutines::store_value_type_fields_to_buf());
5290   } else {
5291     call(RuntimeAddress(StubRoutines::store_value_type_fields_to_buf()));
5292     call_offset = offset();
5293   }
5294 
5295   bind(skip);
5296   return call_offset;
5297 }
5298 
5299 
5300 // Move a value between registers/stack slots and update the reg_state
5301 bool MacroAssembler::move_helper(VMReg from, VMReg to, BasicType bt, RegState reg_state[], int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5302   if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_written) {
5303     return true; // Already written
5304   }
5305   if (from != to && bt != T_VOID) {
5306     if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_readonly) {
5307       return false; // Not yet writable
5308     }
5309     if (from->is_reg()) {
5310       if (to->is_reg()) {
5311         if (from->is_XMMRegister()) {
5312           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5313             movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), from->as_XMMRegister());
5314           } else {
5315             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5316             movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), from->as_XMMRegister());
5317           }
5318         } else {
5319           movq(to->as_Register(), from->as_Register());
5320         }
5321       } else {
5322         int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5323         assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5324         Address to_addr = Address(rsp, st_off);
5325         if (from->is_XMMRegister()) {
5326           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5327             movdbl(to_addr, from->as_XMMRegister());
5328           } else {
5329             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5330             movflt(to_addr, from->as_XMMRegister());
5331           }
5332         } else {
5333           movq(to_addr, from->as_Register());
5334         }
5335       }
5336     } else {
5337       Address from_addr = Address(rsp, from->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset);
5338       if (to->is_reg()) {
5339         if (to->is_XMMRegister()) {
5340           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5341             movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), from_addr);
5342           } else {
5343             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5344             movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), from_addr);
5345           }
5346         } else {
5347           movq(to->as_Register(), from_addr);
5348         }
5349       } else {
5350         int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5351         assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5352         movq(r13, from_addr);
5353         movq(Address(rsp, st_off), r13);
5354       }
5355     }
5356   }
5357   // Update register states
5358   reg_state[from->value()] = reg_writable;
5359   reg_state[to->value()] = reg_written;
5360   return true;
5361 }
5362 
5363 // Read all fields from a value type oop and store the values in registers/stack slots
5364 bool MacroAssembler::unpack_value_helper(const GrowableArray<SigEntry>* sig, int& sig_index, VMReg from, VMRegPair* regs_to,
5365                                          int& to_index, RegState reg_state[], int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5366   Register fromReg = from->is_reg() ? from->as_Register() : noreg;
5367   assert(sig->at(sig_index)._bt == T_VOID, "should be at end delimiter");
5368 
5369   int vt = 1;
5370   bool done = true;
5371   bool mark_done = true;
5372   do {
5373     sig_index--;
5374     BasicType bt = sig->at(sig_index)._bt;
5375     if (bt == T_VALUETYPE) {
5376       vt--;
5377     } else if (bt == T_VOID &&
5378                sig->at(sig_index-1)._bt != T_LONG &&
5379                sig->at(sig_index-1)._bt != T_DOUBLE) {
5380       vt++;
5381     } else if (SigEntry::is_reserved_entry(sig, sig_index)) {
5382       to_index--; // Ignore this
5383     } else {
5384       assert(to_index >= 0, "invalid to_index");
5385       VMRegPair pair_to = regs_to[to_index--];
5386       VMReg to = pair_to.first();
5387 
5388       if (bt == T_VOID) continue;
5389 
5390       int idx = (int)to->value();
5391       if (reg_state[idx] == reg_readonly) {
5392          if (idx != from->value()) {
5393            mark_done = false;
5394          }
5395          done = false;
5396          continue;
5397       } else if (reg_state[idx] == reg_written) {
5398         continue;
5399       } else {
5400         assert(reg_state[idx] == reg_writable, "must be writable");
5401         reg_state[idx] = reg_written;
5402        }
5403 
5404       if (fromReg == noreg) {
5405         int st_off = from->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5406         movq(r10, Address(rsp, st_off));
5407         fromReg = r10;
5408       }
5409 
5410       int off = sig->at(sig_index)._offset;
5411       assert(off > 0, "offset in object should be positive");
5412       bool is_oop = (bt == T_OBJECT || bt == T_ARRAY);
5413 
5414       Address fromAddr = Address(fromReg, off);
5415       bool is_signed = (bt != T_CHAR) && (bt != T_BOOLEAN);
5416       if (!to->is_XMMRegister()) {
5417         Register dst = to->is_stack() ? r13 : to->as_Register();
5418         if (is_oop) {
5419           load_heap_oop(dst, fromAddr);
5420         } else {
5421           load_sized_value(dst, fromAddr, type2aelembytes(bt), is_signed);
5422         }
5423         if (to->is_stack()) {
5424           int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5425           assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5426           movq(Address(rsp, st_off), dst);
5427         }
5428       } else {
5429         if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5430           movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), fromAddr);
5431         } else {
5432           assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5433           movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), fromAddr);
5434         }
5435       }
5436     }
5437   } while (vt != 0);
5438   if (mark_done && reg_state[from->value()] != reg_written) {
5439     // This is okay because no one else will write to that slot
5440     reg_state[from->value()] = reg_writable;
5441   }
5442   return done;
5443 }
5444 
5445 // Pack fields back into a value type oop
5446 bool MacroAssembler::pack_value_helper(const GrowableArray<SigEntry>* sig, int& sig_index, int vtarg_index,
5447                                        VMReg to, VMRegPair* regs_from, int regs_from_count, int& from_index, RegState reg_state[],
5448                                        int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5449   assert(sig->at(sig_index)._bt == T_VALUETYPE, "should be at end delimiter");
5450   assert(to->is_valid(), "must be");
5451 
5452   if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_written) {
5453     skip_unpacked_fields(sig, sig_index, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index);
5454     return true; // Already written
5455   }
5456 
5457   Register val_array = rax;
5458   Register val_obj_tmp = r11;
5459   Register from_reg_tmp = r14; // Be careful with r14 because it's used for spilling
5460   Register tmp1 = r10;
5461   Register tmp2 = r13;
5462   Register tmp3 = rbx;
5463   Register val_obj = to->is_stack() ? val_obj_tmp : to->as_Register();
5464 
5465   if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_readonly) {
5466     if (!is_reg_in_unpacked_fields(sig, sig_index, to, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index)) {
5467       skip_unpacked_fields(sig, sig_index, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index);
5468       return false; // Not yet writable
5469     }
5470     val_obj = val_obj_tmp;
5471   }
5472 
5473   int index = arrayOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes(T_OBJECT) + vtarg_index * type2aelembytes(T_VALUETYPE);
5474   load_heap_oop(val_obj, Address(val_array, index));
5475 
5476   ScalarizedValueArgsStream stream(sig, sig_index, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index);
5477   VMRegPair from_pair;
5478   BasicType bt;
5479   while (stream.next(from_pair, bt)) {
5480     int off = sig->at(stream.sig_cc_index())._offset;
5481     assert(off > 0, "offset in object should be positive");
5482     bool is_oop = (bt == T_OBJECT || bt == T_ARRAY);
5483     size_t size_in_bytes = is_java_primitive(bt) ? type2aelembytes(bt) : wordSize;
5484 
5485     VMReg from_r1 = from_pair.first();
5486     VMReg from_r2 = from_pair.second();
5487 
5488     // Pack the scalarized field into the value object.
5489     Address dst(val_obj, off);
5490     if (!from_r1->is_XMMRegister()) {
5491       Register from_reg;
5492       if (from_r1->is_stack()) {
5493         from_reg = from_reg_tmp;
5494         int ld_off = from_r1->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5495         load_sized_value(from_reg, Address(rsp, ld_off), size_in_bytes, /* is_signed */ false);
5496       } else {
5497         from_reg = from_r1->as_Register();
5498       }
5499       assert_different_registers(dst.base(), from_reg, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, val_array);
5500       if (is_oop) {
5501         store_heap_oop(dst, from_reg, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, IN_HEAP | ACCESS_WRITE | IS_DEST_UNINITIALIZED);
5502       } else {
5503         store_sized_value(dst, from_reg, size_in_bytes);
5504       }
5505     } else {
5506       if (from_r2->is_valid()) {
5507         movdbl(dst, from_r1->as_XMMRegister());
5508       } else {
5509         movflt(dst, from_r1->as_XMMRegister());
5510       }
5511     }
5512     reg_state[from_r1->value()] = reg_writable;
5513   }
5514   sig_index = stream.sig_cc_index();
5515   from_index = stream.regs_cc_index();
5516 
5517   assert(reg_state[to->value()] == reg_writable, "must have already been read");
5518   bool success = move_helper(val_obj->as_VMReg(), to, T_OBJECT, reg_state, ret_off, extra_stack_offset);
5519   assert(success, "to register must be writeable");
5520 
5521   return true;
5522 }
5523 
5524 // Unpack all value type arguments passed as oops
5525 void MacroAssembler::unpack_value_args(Compile* C, bool receiver_only) {
5526   int sp_inc = unpack_value_args_common(C, receiver_only);
5527   // Emit code for verified entry and save increment for stack repair on return
5528   verified_entry(C, sp_inc);
5529 }
5530 
5531 void MacroAssembler::shuffle_value_args(bool is_packing, bool receiver_only, int extra_stack_offset,
5532                                         BasicType* sig_bt, const GrowableArray<SigEntry>* sig_cc,
5533                                         int args_passed, int args_on_stack, VMRegPair* regs,
5534                                         int args_passed_to, int args_on_stack_to, VMRegPair* regs_to, int sp_inc) {
5535   // Check if we need to extend the stack for packing/unpacking
5536   if (sp_inc > 0 && !is_packing) {
5537     // Save the return address, adjust the stack (make sure it is properly
5538     // 16-byte aligned) and copy the return address to the new top of the stack.
5539     // (Note: C1 does this in C1_MacroAssembler::scalarized_entry).
5540     pop(r13);
5541     subptr(rsp, sp_inc);
5542     push(r13);
5543   }
5544 
5545   int ret_off; // make sure we don't overwrite the return address
5546   if (is_packing) {
5547     // For C1 code, the VVEP doesn't have reserved slots, so we store the returned address at
5548     // rsp[0] during shuffling.
5549     ret_off = 0;
5550   } else {
5551     // C2 code ensures that sp_inc is a reserved slot.
5552     ret_off = sp_inc;
5553   }
5554 
5555   shuffle_value_args_common(is_packing, receiver_only, extra_stack_offset,
5556                             sig_bt, sig_cc,
5557                             args_passed, args_on_stack, regs,
5558                             args_passed_to, args_on_stack_to, regs_to,
5559                             sp_inc, ret_off);
5560 }
5561 
5562 VMReg MacroAssembler::spill_reg_for(VMReg reg) {
5563   return reg->is_XMMRegister() ? xmm8->as_VMReg() : r14->as_VMReg();
5564 }
5565 
5566 void MacroAssembler::remove_frame(int initial_framesize, bool needs_stack_repair, int sp_inc_offset) {
5567   assert((initial_framesize & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "frame size not aligned");
5568   if (needs_stack_repair) {
5569     movq(rbp, Address(rsp, initial_framesize));
5570     addq(rsp, Address(rsp, sp_inc_offset));
5571   } else {
5572     if (initial_framesize > 0) {
5573       addq(rsp, initial_framesize);
5574     }
5575     pop(rbp);
5576   }
5577 }
5578 
5579 void MacroAssembler::clear_mem(Register base, Register cnt, Register val, XMMRegister xtmp, bool is_large, bool word_copy_only) {
5580   // cnt - number of qwords (8-byte words).
5581   // base - start address, qword aligned.
5582   // is_large - if optimizers know cnt is larger than InitArrayShortSize
5583   assert(base==rdi, "base register must be edi for rep stos");
5584   assert(val==rax,   "tmp register must be eax for rep stos");
5585   assert(cnt==rcx,   "cnt register must be ecx for rep stos");
5586   assert(InitArrayShortSize % BytesPerLong == 0,
5587     "InitArrayShortSize should be the multiple of BytesPerLong");
5588 
5589   Label DONE;
5590 
5591   if (!is_large) {
5592     Label LOOP, LONG;
5593     cmpptr(cnt, InitArrayShortSize/BytesPerLong);
5594     jccb(Assembler::greater, LONG);
5595 
5596     NOT_LP64(shlptr(cnt, 1);) // convert to number of 32-bit words for 32-bit VM
5597 
5598     decrement(cnt);
5599     jccb(Assembler::negative, DONE); // Zero length
5600 
5601     // Use individual pointer-sized stores for small counts:
5602     BIND(LOOP);
5603     movptr(Address(base, cnt, Address::times_ptr), val);
5604     decrement(cnt);
5605     jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, LOOP);
5606     jmpb(DONE);
5607 
5608     BIND(LONG);
5609   }
5610 
5611   // Use longer rep-prefixed ops for non-small counts:
5612   if (UseFastStosb && !word_copy_only) {
5613     shlptr(cnt, 3); // convert to number of bytes
5614     rep_stosb();
5615   } else if (UseXMMForObjInit) {
5616     xmm_clear_mem(base, cnt, val, xtmp);
5617   } else {
5618     NOT_LP64(shlptr(cnt, 1);) // convert to number of 32-bit words for 32-bit VM
5619     rep_stos();
5620   }
5621 
5622   BIND(DONE);
5623 }
5624 
5625 void MacroAssembler::generate_fill(BasicType t, bool aligned,
5626                                    Register to, Register value, Register count,
5627                                    Register rtmp, XMMRegister xtmp) {
5628   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
5629   assert_different_registers(to, value, count, rtmp);
5630   Label L_exit;
5631   Label L_fill_2_bytes, L_fill_4_bytes;
5632 
5633   int shift = -1;
5634   switch (t) {
5635     case T_BYTE:
5636       shift = 2;
5637       break;
5638     case T_SHORT:
5639       shift = 1;
5640       break;
5641     case T_INT:
5642       shift = 0;
5643       break;
5644     default: ShouldNotReachHere();
5645   }
5646 
5647   if (t == T_BYTE) {
5648     andl(value, 0xff);
5649     movl(rtmp, value);
5650     shll(rtmp, 8);
5651     orl(value, rtmp);
5652   }
5653   if (t == T_SHORT) {
5654     andl(value, 0xffff);
5655   }
5656   if (t == T_BYTE || t == T_SHORT) {
5657     movl(rtmp, value);
5658     shll(rtmp, 16);
5659     orl(value, rtmp);
5660   }
5661 
5662   cmpl(count, 2<<shift); // Short arrays (< 8 bytes) fill by element
5663   jcc(Assembler::below, L_fill_4_bytes); // use unsigned cmp
5664   if (!UseUnalignedLoadStores && !aligned && (t == T_BYTE || t == T_SHORT)) {
5665     Label L_skip_align2;
5666     // align source address at 4 bytes address boundary
5667     if (t == T_BYTE) {
5668       Label L_skip_align1;
5669       // One byte misalignment happens only for byte arrays
5670       testptr(to, 1);
5671       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_skip_align1);
5672       movb(Address(to, 0), value);
5673       increment(to);
5674       decrement(count);
5675       BIND(L_skip_align1);
5676     }
5677     // Two bytes misalignment happens only for byte and short (char) arrays
5678     testptr(to, 2);
5679     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_skip_align2);
5680     movw(Address(to, 0), value);
5681     addptr(to, 2);
5682     subl(count, 1<<(shift-1));
5683     BIND(L_skip_align2);
5684   }
5685   if (UseSSE < 2) {
5686     Label L_fill_32_bytes_loop, L_check_fill_8_bytes, L_fill_8_bytes_loop, L_fill_8_bytes;
5687     // Fill 32-byte chunks
5688     subl(count, 8 << shift);
5689     jcc(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5690     align(16);
5691 
5692     BIND(L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5693 
5694     for (int i = 0; i < 32; i += 4) {
5695       movl(Address(to, i), value);
5696     }
5697 
5698     addptr(to, 32);
5699     subl(count, 8 << shift);
5700     jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5701     BIND(L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5702     addl(count, 8 << shift);
5703     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
5704     jmpb(L_fill_8_bytes);
5705 
5706     //
5707     // length is too short, just fill qwords
5708     //
5709     BIND(L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5710     movl(Address(to, 0), value);
5711     movl(Address(to, 4), value);
5712     addptr(to, 8);
5713     BIND(L_fill_8_bytes);
5714     subl(count, 1 << (shift + 1));
5715     jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5716     // fall through to fill 4 bytes
5717   } else {
5718     Label L_fill_32_bytes;
5719     if (!UseUnalignedLoadStores) {
5720       // align to 8 bytes, we know we are 4 byte aligned to start
5721       testptr(to, 4);
5722       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_fill_32_bytes);
5723       movl(Address(to, 0), value);
5724       addptr(to, 4);
5725       subl(count, 1<<shift);
5726     }
5727     BIND(L_fill_32_bytes);
5728     {
5729       assert( UseSSE >= 2, "supported cpu only" );
5730       Label L_fill_32_bytes_loop, L_check_fill_8_bytes, L_fill_8_bytes_loop, L_fill_8_bytes;
5731       movdl(xtmp, value);
5732       if (UseAVX >= 2 && UseUnalignedLoadStores) {
5733         Label L_check_fill_32_bytes;
5734         if (UseAVX > 2) {
5735           // Fill 64-byte chunks
5736           Label L_fill_64_bytes_loop_avx3, L_check_fill_64_bytes_avx2;
5737 
5738           // If number of bytes to fill < AVX3Threshold, perform fill using AVX2
5739           cmpl(count, AVX3Threshold);
5740           jccb(Assembler::below, L_check_fill_64_bytes_avx2);
5741 
5742           vpbroadcastd(xtmp, xtmp, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
5743 
5744           subl(count, 16 << shift);
5745           jccb(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5746           align(16);
5747 
5748           BIND(L_fill_64_bytes_loop_avx3);
5749           evmovdqul(Address(to, 0), xtmp, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
5750           addptr(to, 64);
5751           subl(count, 16 << shift);
5752           jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_64_bytes_loop_avx3);
5753           jmpb(L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5754 
5755           BIND(L_check_fill_64_bytes_avx2);
5756         }
5757         // Fill 64-byte chunks
5758         Label L_fill_64_bytes_loop;
5759         vpbroadcastd(xtmp, xtmp, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
5760 
5761         subl(count, 16 << shift);
5762         jcc(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5763         align(16);
5764 
5765         BIND(L_fill_64_bytes_loop);
5766         vmovdqu(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5767         vmovdqu(Address(to, 32), xtmp);
5768         addptr(to, 64);
5769         subl(count, 16 << shift);
5770         jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_64_bytes_loop);
5771 
5772         BIND(L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5773         addl(count, 8 << shift);
5774         jccb(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5775         vmovdqu(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5776         addptr(to, 32);
5777         subl(count, 8 << shift);
5778 
5779         BIND(L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5780         // clean upper bits of YMM registers
5781         movdl(xtmp, value);
5782         pshufd(xtmp, xtmp, 0);
5783       } else {
5784         // Fill 32-byte chunks
5785         pshufd(xtmp, xtmp, 0);
5786 
5787         subl(count, 8 << shift);
5788         jcc(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5789         align(16);
5790 
5791         BIND(L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5792 
5793         if (UseUnalignedLoadStores) {
5794           movdqu(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5795           movdqu(Address(to, 16), xtmp);
5796         } else {
5797           movq(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5798           movq(Address(to, 8), xtmp);
5799           movq(Address(to, 16), xtmp);
5800           movq(Address(to, 24), xtmp);
5801         }
5802 
5803         addptr(to, 32);
5804         subl(count, 8 << shift);
5805         jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5806 
5807         BIND(L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5808       }
5809       addl(count, 8 << shift);
5810       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
5811       jmpb(L_fill_8_bytes);
5812 
5813       //
5814       // length is too short, just fill qwords
5815       //
5816       BIND(L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5817       movq(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5818       addptr(to, 8);
5819       BIND(L_fill_8_bytes);
5820       subl(count, 1 << (shift + 1));
5821       jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5822     }
5823   }
5824   // fill trailing 4 bytes
5825   BIND(L_fill_4_bytes);
5826   testl(count, 1<<shift);
5827   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_fill_2_bytes);
5828   movl(Address(to, 0), value);
5829   if (t == T_BYTE || t == T_SHORT) {
5830     Label L_fill_byte;
5831     addptr(to, 4);
5832     BIND(L_fill_2_bytes);
5833     // fill trailing 2 bytes
5834     testl(count, 1<<(shift-1));
5835     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_fill_byte);
5836     movw(Address(to, 0), value);
5837     if (t == T_BYTE) {
5838       addptr(to, 2);
5839       BIND(L_fill_byte);
5840       // fill trailing byte
5841       testl(count, 1);
5842       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
5843       movb(Address(to, 0), value);
5844     } else {
5845       BIND(L_fill_byte);
5846     }
5847   } else {
5848     BIND(L_fill_2_bytes);
5849   }
5850   BIND(L_exit);
5851 }
5852 
5853 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5854    //@HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate
5855    //private static int implEncodeISOArray(byte[] sa, int sp,
5856    //byte[] da, int dp, int len) {
5857    //  int i = 0;
5858    //  for (; i < len; i++) {
5859    //    char c = StringUTF16.getChar(sa, sp++);
5860    //    if (c > '\u00FF')
5861    //      break;
5862    //    da[dp++] = (byte)c;
5863    //  }
5864    //  return i;
5865    //}
5866 void MacroAssembler::encode_iso_array(Register src, Register dst, Register len,
5867   XMMRegister tmp1Reg, XMMRegister tmp2Reg,
5868   XMMRegister tmp3Reg, XMMRegister tmp4Reg,
5869   Register tmp5, Register result) {
5870 
5871   // rsi: src
5872   // rdi: dst
5873   // rdx: len
5874   // rcx: tmp5
5875   // rax: result
5876   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
5877   assert_different_registers(src, dst, len, tmp5, result);
5878   Label L_done, L_copy_1_char, L_copy_1_char_exit;
5879 
5880   // set result
5881   xorl(result, result);
5882   // check for zero length
5883   testl(len, len);
5884   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_done);
5885 
5886   movl(result, len);
5887 
5888   // Setup pointers
5889   lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2)); // char[]
5890   lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1)); // byte[]
5891   negptr(len);
5892 
5893   if (UseSSE42Intrinsics || UseAVX >= 2) {
5894     Label L_copy_8_chars, L_copy_8_chars_exit;
5895     Label L_chars_16_check, L_copy_16_chars, L_copy_16_chars_exit;
5896 
5897     if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5898       Label L_chars_32_check, L_copy_32_chars, L_copy_32_chars_exit;
5899       movl(tmp5, 0xff00ff00);   // create mask to test for Unicode chars in vector
5900       movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
5901       vpbroadcastd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
5902       jmp(L_chars_32_check);
5903 
5904       bind(L_copy_32_chars);
5905       vmovdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -64));
5906       vmovdqu(tmp4Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5907       vpor(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg, /* vector_len */ 1);
5908       vptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in  vector
5909       jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_32_chars_exit);
5910       vpackuswb(tmp3Reg, tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg, /* vector_len */ 1);
5911       vpermq(tmp4Reg, tmp3Reg, 0xD8, /* vector_len */ 1);
5912       vmovdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, -32), tmp4Reg);
5913 
5914       bind(L_chars_32_check);
5915       addptr(len, 32);
5916       jcc(Assembler::lessEqual, L_copy_32_chars);
5917 
5918       bind(L_copy_32_chars_exit);
5919       subptr(len, 16);
5920       jccb(Assembler::greater, L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5921 
5922     } else if (UseSSE42Intrinsics) {
5923       movl(tmp5, 0xff00ff00);   // create mask to test for Unicode chars in vector
5924       movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
5925       pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);
5926       jmpb(L_chars_16_check);
5927     }
5928 
5929     bind(L_copy_16_chars);
5930     if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5931       vmovdqu(tmp2Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5932       vptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);
5933       jcc(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5934       vpackuswb(tmp2Reg, tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg, /* vector_len */ 1);
5935       vpermq(tmp3Reg, tmp2Reg, 0xD8, /* vector_len */ 1);
5936     } else {
5937       if (UseAVX > 0) {
5938         movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5939         movdqu(tmp4Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -16));
5940         vpor(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg, /* vector_len */ 0);
5941       } else {
5942         movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5943         por(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg);
5944         movdqu(tmp4Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -16));
5945         por(tmp2Reg, tmp4Reg);
5946       }
5947       ptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in  vector
5948       jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5949       packuswb(tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg);
5950     }
5951     movdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, -16), tmp3Reg);
5952 
5953     bind(L_chars_16_check);
5954     addptr(len, 16);
5955     jcc(Assembler::lessEqual, L_copy_16_chars);
5956 
5957     bind(L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5958     if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5959       // clean upper bits of YMM registers
5960       vpxor(tmp2Reg, tmp2Reg);
5961       vpxor(tmp3Reg, tmp3Reg);
5962       vpxor(tmp4Reg, tmp4Reg);
5963       movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
5964       pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);
5965     }
5966     subptr(len, 8);
5967     jccb(Assembler::greater, L_copy_8_chars_exit);
5968 
5969     bind(L_copy_8_chars);
5970     movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -16));
5971     ptest(tmp3Reg, tmp1Reg);
5972     jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_8_chars_exit);
5973     packuswb(tmp3Reg, tmp1Reg);
5974     movq(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, -8), tmp3Reg);
5975     addptr(len, 8);
5976     jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_copy_8_chars);
5977 
5978     bind(L_copy_8_chars_exit);
5979     subptr(len, 8);
5980     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_done);
5981   }
5982 
5983   bind(L_copy_1_char);
5984   load_unsigned_short(tmp5, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, 0));
5985   testl(tmp5, 0xff00);      // check if Unicode char
5986   jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_1_char_exit);
5987   movb(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, 0), tmp5);
5988   addptr(len, 1);
5989   jccb(Assembler::less, L_copy_1_char);
5990 
5991   bind(L_copy_1_char_exit);
5992   addptr(result, len); // len is negative count of not processed elements
5993 
5994   bind(L_done);
5995 }

5997 #ifdef _LP64
5998 /**
5999  * Helper for multiply_to_len().
6000  */
6001 void MacroAssembler::add2_with_carry(Register dest_hi, Register dest_lo, Register src1, Register src2) {
6002   addq(dest_lo, src1);
6003   adcq(dest_hi, 0);
6004   addq(dest_lo, src2);
6005   adcq(dest_hi, 0);
6006 }
6007 
6008 /**
6009  * Multiply 64 bit by 64 bit first loop.
6010  */
6011 void MacroAssembler::multiply_64_x_64_loop(Register x, Register xstart, Register x_xstart,
6012                                            Register y, Register y_idx, Register z,
6013                                            Register carry, Register product,
6014                                            Register idx, Register kdx) {
6015   //
6016   //  jlong carry, x[], y[], z[];
6017   //  for (int idx=ystart, kdx=ystart+1+xstart; idx >= 0; idx-, kdx--) {
6018   //    huge_128 product = y[idx] * x[xstart] + carry;
6019   //    z[kdx] = (jlong)product;
6020   //    carry  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6021   //  }
6022   //  z[xstart] = carry;
6023   //
6024 
6025   Label L_first_loop, L_first_loop_exit;
6026   Label L_one_x, L_one_y, L_multiply;
6027 
6028   decrementl(xstart);
6029   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_one_x);
6030 
6031   movq(x_xstart, Address(x, xstart, Address::times_4,  0));
6032   rorq(x_xstart, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6033 
6034   bind(L_first_loop);
6035   decrementl(idx);
6036   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_first_loop_exit);
6037   decrementl(idx);
6038   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_one_y);
6039   movq(y_idx, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6040   rorq(y_idx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6041   bind(L_multiply);
6042   movq(product, x_xstart);
6043   mulq(y_idx); // product(rax) * y_idx -> rdx:rax
6044   addq(product, carry);
6045   adcq(rdx, 0);
6046   subl(kdx, 2);
6047   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  4), product);
6048   shrq(product, 32);
6049   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  0), product);
6050   movq(carry, rdx);
6051   jmp(L_first_loop);
6052 
6053   bind(L_one_y);
6054   movl(y_idx, Address(y,  0));
6055   jmp(L_multiply);
6056 
6057   bind(L_one_x);
6058   movl(x_xstart, Address(x,  0));
6059   jmp(L_first_loop);
6060 
6061   bind(L_first_loop_exit);
6062 }
6063 
6064 /**
6065  * Multiply 64 bit by 64 bit and add 128 bit.
6066  */
6067 void MacroAssembler::multiply_add_128_x_128(Register x_xstart, Register y, Register z,
6068                                             Register yz_idx, Register idx,
6069                                             Register carry, Register product, int offset) {
6070   //     huge_128 product = (y[idx] * x_xstart) + z[kdx] + carry;
6071   //     z[kdx] = (jlong)product;
6072 
6073   movq(yz_idx, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  offset));
6074   rorq(yz_idx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6075   movq(product, x_xstart);
6076   mulq(yz_idx);     // product(rax) * yz_idx -> rdx:product(rax)
6077   movq(yz_idx, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  offset));
6078   rorq(yz_idx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6079 
6080   add2_with_carry(rdx, product, carry, yz_idx);
6081 
6082   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  offset+4), product);
6083   shrq(product, 32);
6084   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  offset), product);
6085 
6086 }
6087 
6088 /**
6089  * Multiply 128 bit by 128 bit. Unrolled inner loop.
6090  */
6091 void MacroAssembler::multiply_128_x_128_loop(Register x_xstart, Register y, Register z,
6092                                              Register yz_idx, Register idx, Register jdx,
6093                                              Register carry, Register product,
6094                                              Register carry2) {
6095   //   jlong carry, x[], y[], z[];
6096   //   int kdx = ystart+1;
6097   //   for (int idx=ystart-2; idx >= 0; idx -= 2) { // Third loop
6098   //     huge_128 product = (y[idx+1] * x_xstart) + z[kdx+idx+1] + carry;
6099   //     z[kdx+idx+1] = (jlong)product;
6100   //     jlong carry2  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6101   //     product = (y[idx] * x_xstart) + z[kdx+idx] + carry2;
6102   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)product;
6103   //     carry  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6104   //   }
6105   //   idx += 2;
6106   //   if (idx > 0) {
6107   //     product = (y[idx] * x_xstart) + z[kdx+idx] + carry;
6108   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)product;
6109   //     carry  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6110   //   }
6111   //
6112 
6113   Label L_third_loop, L_third_loop_exit, L_post_third_loop_done;
6114 
6115   movl(jdx, idx);
6116   andl(jdx, 0xFFFFFFFC);
6117   shrl(jdx, 2);
6118 
6119   bind(L_third_loop);
6120   subl(jdx, 1);
6121   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_third_loop_exit);
6122   subl(idx, 4);
6123 
6124   multiply_add_128_x_128(x_xstart, y, z, yz_idx, idx, carry, product, 8);
6125   movq(carry2, rdx);
6126 
6127   multiply_add_128_x_128(x_xstart, y, z, yz_idx, idx, carry2, product, 0);
6128   movq(carry, rdx);
6129   jmp(L_third_loop);
6130 
6131   bind (L_third_loop_exit);
6132 
6133   andl (idx, 0x3);
6134   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_post_third_loop_done);
6135 
6136   Label L_check_1;
6137   subl(idx, 2);
6138   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_check_1);
6139 
6140   multiply_add_128_x_128(x_xstart, y, z, yz_idx, idx, carry, product, 0);
6141   movq(carry, rdx);
6142 
6143   bind (L_check_1);
6144   addl (idx, 0x2);
6145   andl (idx, 0x1);
6146   subl(idx, 1);
6147   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_post_third_loop_done);
6148 
6149   movl(yz_idx, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6150   movq(product, x_xstart);
6151   mulq(yz_idx); // product(rax) * yz_idx -> rdx:product(rax)
6152   movl(yz_idx, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6153 
6154   add2_with_carry(rdx, product, yz_idx, carry);
6155 
6156   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), product);
6157   shrq(product, 32);
6158 
6159   shlq(rdx, 32);
6160   orq(product, rdx);
6161   movq(carry, product);
6162 
6163   bind(L_post_third_loop_done);
6164 }
6165 
6166 /**
6167  * Multiply 128 bit by 128 bit using BMI2. Unrolled inner loop.
6168  *
6169  */
6170 void MacroAssembler::multiply_128_x_128_bmi2_loop(Register y, Register z,
6171                                                   Register carry, Register carry2,
6172                                                   Register idx, Register jdx,
6173                                                   Register yz_idx1, Register yz_idx2,
6174                                                   Register tmp, Register tmp3, Register tmp4) {
6175   assert(UseBMI2Instructions, "should be used only when BMI2 is available");
6176 
6177   //   jlong carry, x[], y[], z[];
6178   //   int kdx = ystart+1;
6179   //   for (int idx=ystart-2; idx >= 0; idx -= 2) { // Third loop
6180   //     huge_128 tmp3 = (y[idx+1] * rdx) + z[kdx+idx+1] + carry;
6181   //     jlong carry2  = (jlong)(tmp3 >>> 64);
6182   //     huge_128 tmp4 = (y[idx]   * rdx) + z[kdx+idx] + carry2;
6183   //     carry  = (jlong)(tmp4 >>> 64);
6184   //     z[kdx+idx+1] = (jlong)tmp3;
6185   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)tmp4;
6186   //   }
6187   //   idx += 2;
6188   //   if (idx > 0) {
6189   //     yz_idx1 = (y[idx] * rdx) + z[kdx+idx] + carry;
6190   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)yz_idx1;
6191   //     carry  = (jlong)(yz_idx1 >>> 64);
6192   //   }
6193   //
6194 
6195   Label L_third_loop, L_third_loop_exit, L_post_third_loop_done;
6196 
6197   movl(jdx, idx);
6198   andl(jdx, 0xFFFFFFFC);
6199   shrl(jdx, 2);
6200 
6201   bind(L_third_loop);
6202   subl(jdx, 1);
6203   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_third_loop_exit);
6204   subl(idx, 4);
6205 
6206   movq(yz_idx1,  Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  8));
6207   rorxq(yz_idx1, yz_idx1, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6208   movq(yz_idx2, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6209   rorxq(yz_idx2, yz_idx2, 32);
6210 
6211   mulxq(tmp4, tmp3, yz_idx1);  //  yz_idx1 * rdx -> tmp4:tmp3
6212   mulxq(carry2, tmp, yz_idx2); //  yz_idx2 * rdx -> carry2:tmp
6213 
6214   movq(yz_idx1,  Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  8));
6215   rorxq(yz_idx1, yz_idx1, 32);
6216   movq(yz_idx2, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6217   rorxq(yz_idx2, yz_idx2, 32);
6218 
6219   if (VM_Version::supports_adx()) {
6220     adcxq(tmp3, carry);
6221     adoxq(tmp3, yz_idx1);
6222 
6223     adcxq(tmp4, tmp);
6224     adoxq(tmp4, yz_idx2);
6225 
6226     movl(carry, 0); // does not affect flags
6227     adcxq(carry2, carry);
6228     adoxq(carry2, carry);
6229   } else {
6230     add2_with_carry(tmp4, tmp3, carry, yz_idx1);
6231     add2_with_carry(carry2, tmp4, tmp, yz_idx2);
6232   }
6233   movq(carry, carry2);
6234 
6235   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4, 12), tmp3);
6236   shrq(tmp3, 32);
6237   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  8), tmp3);
6238 
6239   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  4), tmp4);
6240   shrq(tmp4, 32);
6241   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), tmp4);
6242 
6243   jmp(L_third_loop);
6244 
6245   bind (L_third_loop_exit);
6246 
6247   andl (idx, 0x3);
6248   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_post_third_loop_done);
6249 
6250   Label L_check_1;
6251   subl(idx, 2);
6252   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_check_1);
6253 
6254   movq(yz_idx1, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6255   rorxq(yz_idx1, yz_idx1, 32);
6256   mulxq(tmp4, tmp3, yz_idx1); //  yz_idx1 * rdx -> tmp4:tmp3
6257   movq(yz_idx2, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6258   rorxq(yz_idx2, yz_idx2, 32);
6259 
6260   add2_with_carry(tmp4, tmp3, carry, yz_idx2);
6261 
6262   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  4), tmp3);
6263   shrq(tmp3, 32);
6264   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), tmp3);
6265   movq(carry, tmp4);
6266 
6267   bind (L_check_1);
6268   addl (idx, 0x2);
6269   andl (idx, 0x1);
6270   subl(idx, 1);
6271   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_post_third_loop_done);
6272   movl(tmp4, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6273   mulxq(carry2, tmp3, tmp4);  //  tmp4 * rdx -> carry2:tmp3
6274   movl(tmp4, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6275 
6276   add2_with_carry(carry2, tmp3, tmp4, carry);
6277 
6278   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), tmp3);
6279   shrq(tmp3, 32);
6280 
6281   shlq(carry2, 32);
6282   orq(tmp3, carry2);
6283   movq(carry, tmp3);
6284 
6285   bind(L_post_third_loop_done);
6286 }
6287 
6288 /**
6289  * Code for BigInteger::multiplyToLen() instrinsic.
6290  *
6291  * rdi: x
6292  * rax: xlen
6293  * rsi: y
6294  * rcx: ylen
6295  * r8:  z
6296  * r11: zlen
6297  * r12: tmp1
6298  * r13: tmp2
6299  * r14: tmp3
6300  * r15: tmp4
6301  * rbx: tmp5
6302  *
6303  */
6304 void MacroAssembler::multiply_to_len(Register x, Register xlen, Register y, Register ylen, Register z, Register zlen,
6305                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3, Register tmp4, Register tmp5) {
6306   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
6307   assert_different_registers(x, xlen, y, ylen, z, zlen, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, tmp4, tmp5, rdx);
6308 
6309   push(tmp1);
6310   push(tmp2);
6311   push(tmp3);
6312   push(tmp4);
6313   push(tmp5);
6314 
6315   push(xlen);
6316   push(zlen);
6317 
6318   const Register idx = tmp1;
6319   const Register kdx = tmp2;
6320   const Register xstart = tmp3;
6321 
6322   const Register y_idx = tmp4;
6323   const Register carry = tmp5;
6324   const Register product  = xlen;
6325   const Register x_xstart = zlen;  // reuse register
6326 
6327   // First Loop.
6328   //
6329   //  final static long LONG_MASK = 0xffffffffL;
6330   //  int xstart = xlen - 1;
6331   //  int ystart = ylen - 1;
6332   //  long carry = 0;
6333   //  for (int idx=ystart, kdx=ystart+1+xstart; idx >= 0; idx-, kdx--) {
6334   //    long product = (y[idx] & LONG_MASK) * (x[xstart] & LONG_MASK) + carry;
6335   //    z[kdx] = (int)product;
6336   //    carry = product >>> 32;
6337   //  }
6338   //  z[xstart] = (int)carry;
6339   //
6340 
6341   movl(idx, ylen);      // idx = ylen;
6342   movl(kdx, zlen);      // kdx = xlen+ylen;
6343   xorq(carry, carry);   // carry = 0;
6344 
6345   Label L_done;
6346 
6347   movl(xstart, xlen);
6348   decrementl(xstart);
6349   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_done);
6350 
6351   multiply_64_x_64_loop(x, xstart, x_xstart, y, y_idx, z, carry, product, idx, kdx);
6352 
6353   Label L_second_loop;
6354   testl(kdx, kdx);
6355   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_second_loop);
6356 
6357   Label L_carry;
6358   subl(kdx, 1);
6359   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_carry);
6360 
6361   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6362   shrq(carry, 32);
6363   subl(kdx, 1);
6364 
6365   bind(L_carry);
6366   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6367 
6368   // Second and third (nested) loops.
6369   //
6370   // for (int i = xstart-1; i >= 0; i--) { // Second loop
6371   //   carry = 0;
6372   //   for (int jdx=ystart, k=ystart+1+i; jdx >= 0; jdx--, k--) { // Third loop
6373   //     long product = (y[jdx] & LONG_MASK) * (x[i] & LONG_MASK) +
6374   //                    (z[k] & LONG_MASK) + carry;
6375   //     z[k] = (int)product;
6376   //     carry = product >>> 32;
6377   //   }
6378   //   z[i] = (int)carry;
6379   // }
6380   //
6381   // i = xlen, j = tmp1, k = tmp2, carry = tmp5, x[i] = rdx
6382 
6383   const Register jdx = tmp1;
6384 
6385   bind(L_second_loop);
6386   xorl(carry, carry);    // carry = 0;
6387   movl(jdx, ylen);       // j = ystart+1
6388 
6389   subl(xstart, 1);       // i = xstart-1;
6390   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_done);
6391 
6392   push (z);
6393 
6394   Label L_last_x;
6395   lea(z, Address(z, xstart, Address::times_4, 4)); // z = z + k - j
6396   subl(xstart, 1);       // i = xstart-1;
6397   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_last_x);
6398 
6399   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6400     movq(rdx,  Address(x, xstart, Address::times_4,  0));
6401     rorxq(rdx, rdx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6402   } else {
6403     movq(x_xstart, Address(x, xstart, Address::times_4,  0));
6404     rorq(x_xstart, 32);  // convert big-endian to little-endian
6405   }
6406 
6407   Label L_third_loop_prologue;
6408   bind(L_third_loop_prologue);
6409 
6410   push (x);
6411   push (xstart);
6412   push (ylen);
6413 
6414 
6415   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6416     multiply_128_x_128_bmi2_loop(y, z, carry, x, jdx, ylen, product, tmp2, x_xstart, tmp3, tmp4);
6417   } else { // !UseBMI2Instructions
6418     multiply_128_x_128_loop(x_xstart, y, z, y_idx, jdx, ylen, carry, product, x);
6419   }
6420 
6421   pop(ylen);
6422   pop(xlen);
6423   pop(x);
6424   pop(z);
6425 
6426   movl(tmp3, xlen);
6427   addl(tmp3, 1);
6428   movl(Address(z, tmp3, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6429   subl(tmp3, 1);
6430   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_done);
6431 
6432   shrq(carry, 32);
6433   movl(Address(z, tmp3, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6434   jmp(L_second_loop);
6435 
6436   // Next infrequent code is moved outside loops.
6437   bind(L_last_x);
6438   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6439     movl(rdx, Address(x,  0));
6440   } else {
6441     movl(x_xstart, Address(x,  0));
6442   }
6443   jmp(L_third_loop_prologue);
6444 
6445   bind(L_done);
6446 
6447   pop(zlen);
6448   pop(xlen);
6449 
6450   pop(tmp5);
6451   pop(tmp4);
6452   pop(tmp3);
6453   pop(tmp2);
6454   pop(tmp1);
6455 }
6456 
6457 void MacroAssembler::vectorized_mismatch(Register obja, Register objb, Register length, Register log2_array_indxscale,
6458   Register result, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, XMMRegister rymm0, XMMRegister rymm1, XMMRegister rymm2){
6459   assert(UseSSE42Intrinsics, "SSE4.2 must be enabled.");
6460   Label VECTOR16_LOOP, VECTOR8_LOOP, VECTOR4_LOOP;
6461   Label VECTOR8_TAIL, VECTOR4_TAIL;
6462   Label VECTOR32_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR8_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR4_NOT_EQUAL;
6463   Label SAME_TILL_END, DONE;
6464   Label BYTES_LOOP, BYTES_TAIL, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL;
6465 
6466   //scale is in rcx in both Win64 and Unix
6467   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
6468 
6469   shlq(length);
6470   xorq(result, result);
6471 
6472   if ((AVX3Threshold == 0) && (UseAVX > 2) &&
6473       VM_Version::supports_avx512vlbw()) {
6474     Label VECTOR64_LOOP, VECTOR64_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR32_TAIL;
6475 
6476     cmpq(length, 64);
6477     jcc(Assembler::less, VECTOR32_TAIL);
6478 
6479     movq(tmp1, length);
6480     andq(tmp1, 0x3F);      // tail count
6481     andq(length, ~(0x3F)); //vector count
6482 
6483     bind(VECTOR64_LOOP);
6484     // AVX512 code to compare 64 byte vectors.
6485     evmovdqub(rymm0, Address(obja, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6486     evpcmpeqb(k7, rymm0, Address(objb, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6487     kortestql(k7, k7);
6488     jcc(Assembler::aboveEqual, VECTOR64_NOT_EQUAL);     // mismatch
6489     addq(result, 64);
6490     subq(length, 64);
6491     jccb(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR64_LOOP);
6492 
6493     //bind(VECTOR64_TAIL);
6494     testq(tmp1, tmp1);
6495     jcc(Assembler::zero, SAME_TILL_END);
6496 
6497     //bind(VECTOR64_TAIL);
6498     // AVX512 code to compare upto 63 byte vectors.
6499     mov64(tmp2, 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF);
6500     shlxq(tmp2, tmp2, tmp1);
6501     notq(tmp2);
6502     kmovql(k3, tmp2);
6503 
6504     evmovdqub(rymm0, k3, Address(obja, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6505     evpcmpeqb(k7, k3, rymm0, Address(objb, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6506 
6507     ktestql(k7, k3);
6508     jcc(Assembler::below, SAME_TILL_END);     // not mismatch
6509 
6510     bind(VECTOR64_NOT_EQUAL);
6511     kmovql(tmp1, k7);
6512     notq(tmp1);
6513     tzcntq(tmp1, tmp1);
6514     addq(result, tmp1);
6515     shrq(result);
6516     jmp(DONE);
6517     bind(VECTOR32_TAIL);
6518   }
6519 
6520   cmpq(length, 8);
6521   jcc(Assembler::equal, VECTOR8_LOOP);
6522   jcc(Assembler::less, VECTOR4_TAIL);
6523 
6524   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
6525     Label VECTOR16_TAIL, VECTOR32_LOOP;
6526 
6527     cmpq(length, 16);
6528     jcc(Assembler::equal, VECTOR16_LOOP);
6529     jcc(Assembler::less, VECTOR8_LOOP);
6530 
6531     cmpq(length, 32);
6532     jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR16_TAIL);
6533 
6534     subq(length, 32);
6535     bind(VECTOR32_LOOP);
6536     vmovdqu(rymm0, Address(obja, result));
6537     vmovdqu(rymm1, Address(objb, result));
6538     vpxor(rymm2, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6539     vptest(rymm2, rymm2);
6540     jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR32_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6541     addq(result, 32);
6542     subq(length, 32);
6543     jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, VECTOR32_LOOP);
6544     addq(length, 32);
6545     jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6546     //falling through if less than 32 bytes left //close the branch here.
6547 
6548     bind(VECTOR16_TAIL);
6549     cmpq(length, 16);
6550     jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR8_TAIL);
6551     bind(VECTOR16_LOOP);
6552     movdqu(rymm0, Address(obja, result));
6553     movdqu(rymm1, Address(objb, result));
6554     vpxor(rymm2, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_128bit);
6555     ptest(rymm2, rymm2);
6556     jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6557     addq(result, 16);
6558     subq(length, 16);
6559     jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6560     //falling through if less than 16 bytes left
6561   } else {//regular intrinsics
6562 
6563     cmpq(length, 16);
6564     jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR8_TAIL);
6565 
6566     subq(length, 16);
6567     bind(VECTOR16_LOOP);
6568     movdqu(rymm0, Address(obja, result));
6569     movdqu(rymm1, Address(objb, result));
6570     pxor(rymm0, rymm1);
6571     ptest(rymm0, rymm0);
6572     jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6573     addq(result, 16);
6574     subq(length, 16);
6575     jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, VECTOR16_LOOP);
6576     addq(length, 16);
6577     jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6578     //falling through if less than 16 bytes left
6579   }
6580 
6581   bind(VECTOR8_TAIL);
6582   cmpq(length, 8);
6583   jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR4_TAIL);
6584   bind(VECTOR8_LOOP);
6585   movq(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6586   movq(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6587   xorq(tmp1, tmp2);
6588   testq(tmp1, tmp1);
6589   jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR8_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6590   addq(result, 8);
6591   subq(length, 8);
6592   jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6593   //falling through if less than 8 bytes left
6594 
6595   bind(VECTOR4_TAIL);
6596   cmpq(length, 4);
6597   jccb(Assembler::less, BYTES_TAIL);
6598   bind(VECTOR4_LOOP);
6599   movl(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6600   xorl(tmp1, Address(objb, result));
6601   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6602   jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR4_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6603   addq(result, 4);
6604   subq(length, 4);
6605   jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6606   //falling through if less than 4 bytes left
6607 
6608   bind(BYTES_TAIL);
6609   bind(BYTES_LOOP);
6610   load_unsigned_byte(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6611   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6612   xorl(tmp1, tmp2);
6613   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6614   jcc(Assembler::notZero, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6615   decq(length);
6616   jcc(Assembler::zero, SAME_TILL_END);
6617   incq(result);
6618   load_unsigned_byte(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6619   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6620   xorl(tmp1, tmp2);
6621   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6622   jcc(Assembler::notZero, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6623   decq(length);
6624   jcc(Assembler::zero, SAME_TILL_END);
6625   incq(result);
6626   load_unsigned_byte(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6627   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6628   xorl(tmp1, tmp2);
6629   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6630   jcc(Assembler::notZero, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6631   jmp(SAME_TILL_END);
6632 
6633   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
6634     bind(VECTOR32_NOT_EQUAL);
6635     vpcmpeqb(rymm2, rymm2, rymm2, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6636     vpcmpeqb(rymm0, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6637     vpxor(rymm0, rymm0, rymm2, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6638     vpmovmskb(tmp1, rymm0);
6639     bsfq(tmp1, tmp1);
6640     addq(result, tmp1);
6641     shrq(result);
6642     jmp(DONE);
6643   }
6644 
6645   bind(VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL);
6646   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
6647     vpcmpeqb(rymm2, rymm2, rymm2, Assembler::AVX_128bit);
6648     vpcmpeqb(rymm0, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_128bit);
6649     pxor(rymm0, rymm2);
6650   } else {
6651     pcmpeqb(rymm2, rymm2);
6652     pxor(rymm0, rymm1);
6653     pcmpeqb(rymm0, rymm1);
6654     pxor(rymm0, rymm2);
6655   }
6656   pmovmskb(tmp1, rymm0);
6657   bsfq(tmp1, tmp1);
6658   addq(result, tmp1);
6659   shrq(result);
6660   jmpb(DONE);
6661 
6662   bind(VECTOR8_NOT_EQUAL);
6663   bind(VECTOR4_NOT_EQUAL);
6664   bsfq(tmp1, tmp1);
6665   shrq(tmp1, 3);
6666   addq(result, tmp1);
6667   bind(BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);
6668   shrq(result);
6669   jmpb(DONE);
6670 
6671   bind(SAME_TILL_END);
6672   mov64(result, -1);
6673 
6674   bind(DONE);
6675 }
6676 
6677 //Helper functions for square_to_len()
6678 
6679 /**
6680  * Store the squares of x[], right shifted one bit (divided by 2) into z[]
6681  * Preserves x and z and modifies rest of the registers.
6682  */
6683 void MacroAssembler::square_rshift(Register x, Register xlen, Register z, Register tmp1, Register tmp3, Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
6684   // Perform square and right shift by 1
6685   // Handle odd xlen case first, then for even xlen do the following
6686   // jlong carry = 0;
6687   // for (int j=0, i=0; j < xlen; j+=2, i+=4) {
6688   //     huge_128 product = x[j:j+1] * x[j:j+1];
6689   //     z[i:i+1] = (carry << 63) | (jlong)(product >>> 65);
6690   //     z[i+2:i+3] = (jlong)(product >>> 1);
6691   //     carry = (jlong)product;
6692   // }
6693 
6694   xorq(tmp5, tmp5);     // carry
6695   xorq(rdxReg, rdxReg);
6696   xorl(tmp1, tmp1);     // index for x
6697   xorl(tmp4, tmp4);     // index for z
6698 
6699   Label L_first_loop, L_first_loop_exit;
6700 
6701   testl(xlen, 1);
6702   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_first_loop); //jump if xlen is even
6703 
6704   // Square and right shift by 1 the odd element using 32 bit multiply
6705   movl(raxReg, Address(x, tmp1, Address::times_4, 0));
6706   imulq(raxReg, raxReg);
6707   shrq(raxReg, 1);
6708   adcq(tmp5, 0);
6709   movq(Address(z, tmp4, Address::times_4, 0), raxReg);
6710   incrementl(tmp1);
6711   addl(tmp4, 2);
6712 
6713   // Square and  right shift by 1 the rest using 64 bit multiply
6714   bind(L_first_loop);
6715   cmpptr(tmp1, xlen);
6716   jccb(Assembler::equal, L_first_loop_exit);
6717 
6718   // Square
6719   movq(raxReg, Address(x, tmp1, Address::times_4,  0));
6720   rorq(raxReg, 32);    // convert big-endian to little-endian
6721   mulq(raxReg);        // 64-bit multiply rax * rax -> rdx:rax
6722 
6723   // Right shift by 1 and save carry
6724   shrq(tmp5, 1);       // rdx:rax:tmp5 = (tmp5:rdx:rax) >>> 1
6725   rcrq(rdxReg, 1);
6726   rcrq(raxReg, 1);
6727   adcq(tmp5, 0);
6728 
6729   // Store result in z
6730   movq(Address(z, tmp4, Address::times_4, 0), rdxReg);
6731   movq(Address(z, tmp4, Address::times_4, 8), raxReg);
6732 
6733   // Update indices for x and z
6734   addl(tmp1, 2);
6735   addl(tmp4, 4);
6736   jmp(L_first_loop);
6737 
6738   bind(L_first_loop_exit);
6739 }
6740 
6741 
6742 /**
6743  * Perform the following multiply add operation using BMI2 instructions
6744  * carry:sum = sum + op1*op2 + carry
6745  * op2 should be in rdx
6746  * op2 is preserved, all other registers are modified
6747  */
6748 void MacroAssembler::multiply_add_64_bmi2(Register sum, Register op1, Register op2, Register carry, Register tmp2) {
6749   // assert op2 is rdx
6750   mulxq(tmp2, op1, op1);  //  op1 * op2 -> tmp2:op1
6751   addq(sum, carry);
6752   adcq(tmp2, 0);
6753   addq(sum, op1);
6754   adcq(tmp2, 0);
6755   movq(carry, tmp2);
6756 }
6757 
6758 /**
6759  * Perform the following multiply add operation:
6760  * carry:sum = sum + op1*op2 + carry
6761  * Preserves op1, op2 and modifies rest of registers
6762  */
6763 void MacroAssembler::multiply_add_64(Register sum, Register op1, Register op2, Register carry, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
6764   // rdx:rax = op1 * op2
6765   movq(raxReg, op2);
6766   mulq(op1);
6767 
6768   //  rdx:rax = sum + carry + rdx:rax
6769   addq(sum, carry);
6770   adcq(rdxReg, 0);
6771   addq(sum, raxReg);
6772   adcq(rdxReg, 0);
6773 
6774   // carry:sum = rdx:sum
6775   movq(carry, rdxReg);
6776 }
6777 
6778 /**
6779  * Add 64 bit long carry into z[] with carry propogation.
6780  * Preserves z and carry register values and modifies rest of registers.
6781  *
6782  */
6783 void MacroAssembler::add_one_64(Register z, Register zlen, Register carry, Register tmp1) {
6784   Label L_fourth_loop, L_fourth_loop_exit;
6785 
6786   movl(tmp1, 1);
6787   subl(zlen, 2);
6788   addq(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4, 0), carry);
6789 
6790   bind(L_fourth_loop);
6791   jccb(Assembler::carryClear, L_fourth_loop_exit);
6792   subl(zlen, 2);
6793   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_fourth_loop_exit);
6794   addq(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4, 0), tmp1);
6795   jmp(L_fourth_loop);
6796   bind(L_fourth_loop_exit);
6797 }
6798 
6799 /**
6800  * Shift z[] left by 1 bit.
6801  * Preserves x, len, z and zlen registers and modifies rest of the registers.
6802  *
6803  */
6804 void MacroAssembler::lshift_by_1(Register x, Register len, Register z, Register zlen, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3, Register tmp4) {
6805 
6806   Label L_fifth_loop, L_fifth_loop_exit;
6807 
6808   // Fifth loop
6809   // Perform primitiveLeftShift(z, zlen, 1)
6810 
6811   const Register prev_carry = tmp1;
6812   const Register new_carry = tmp4;
6813   const Register value = tmp2;
6814   const Register zidx = tmp3;
6815 
6816   // int zidx, carry;
6817   // long value;
6818   // carry = 0;
6819   // for (zidx = zlen-2; zidx >=0; zidx -= 2) {
6820   //    (carry:value)  = (z[i] << 1) | carry ;
6821   //    z[i] = value;
6822   // }
6823 
6824   movl(zidx, zlen);
6825   xorl(prev_carry, prev_carry); // clear carry flag and prev_carry register
6826 
6827   bind(L_fifth_loop);
6828   decl(zidx);  // Use decl to preserve carry flag
6829   decl(zidx);
6830   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_fifth_loop_exit);
6831 
6832   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6833      movq(value, Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4, 0));
6834      rclq(value, 1);
6835      rorxq(value, value, 32);
6836      movq(Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4,  0), value);  // Store back in big endian form
6837   }
6838   else {
6839     // clear new_carry
6840     xorl(new_carry, new_carry);
6841 
6842     // Shift z[i] by 1, or in previous carry and save new carry
6843     movq(value, Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4, 0));
6844     shlq(value, 1);
6845     adcl(new_carry, 0);
6846 
6847     orq(value, prev_carry);
6848     rorq(value, 0x20);
6849     movq(Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4,  0), value);  // Store back in big endian form
6850 
6851     // Set previous carry = new carry
6852     movl(prev_carry, new_carry);
6853   }
6854   jmp(L_fifth_loop);
6855 
6856   bind(L_fifth_loop_exit);
6857 }
6858 
6859 
6860 /**
6861  * Code for BigInteger::squareToLen() intrinsic
6862  *
6863  * rdi: x
6864  * rsi: len
6865  * r8:  z
6866  * rcx: zlen
6867  * r12: tmp1
6868  * r13: tmp2
6869  * r14: tmp3
6870  * r15: tmp4
6871  * rbx: tmp5
6872  *
6873  */
6874 void MacroAssembler::square_to_len(Register x, Register len, Register z, Register zlen, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3, Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
6875 
6876   Label L_second_loop, L_second_loop_exit, L_third_loop, L_third_loop_exit, L_last_x, L_multiply;
6877   push(tmp1);
6878   push(tmp2);
6879   push(tmp3);
6880   push(tmp4);
6881   push(tmp5);
6882 
6883   // First loop
6884   // Store the squares, right shifted one bit (i.e., divided by 2).
6885   square_rshift(x, len, z, tmp1, tmp3, tmp4, tmp5, rdxReg, raxReg);
6886 
6887   // Add in off-diagonal sums.
6888   //
6889   // Second, third (nested) and fourth loops.
6890   // zlen +=2;
6891   // for (int xidx=len-2,zidx=zlen-4; xidx > 0; xidx-=2,zidx-=4) {
6892   //    carry = 0;
6893   //    long op2 = x[xidx:xidx+1];
6894   //    for (int j=xidx-2,k=zidx; j >= 0; j-=2) {
6895   //       k -= 2;
6896   //       long op1 = x[j:j+1];
6897   //       long sum = z[k:k+1];
6898   //       carry:sum = multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, tmp_regs);
6899   //       z[k:k+1] = sum;
6900   //    }
6901   //    add_one_64(z, k, carry, tmp_regs);
6902   // }
6903 
6904   const Register carry = tmp5;
6905   const Register sum = tmp3;
6906   const Register op1 = tmp4;
6907   Register op2 = tmp2;
6908 
6909   push(zlen);
6910   push(len);
6911   addl(zlen,2);
6912   bind(L_second_loop);
6913   xorq(carry, carry);
6914   subl(zlen, 4);
6915   subl(len, 2);
6916   push(zlen);
6917   push(len);
6918   cmpl(len, 0);
6919   jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_second_loop_exit);
6920 
6921   // Multiply an array by one 64 bit long.
6922   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6923     op2 = rdxReg;
6924     movq(op2, Address(x, len, Address::times_4,  0));
6925     rorxq(op2, op2, 32);
6926   }
6927   else {
6928     movq(op2, Address(x, len, Address::times_4,  0));
6929     rorq(op2, 32);
6930   }
6931 
6932   bind(L_third_loop);
6933   decrementl(len);
6934   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_third_loop_exit);
6935   decrementl(len);
6936   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_last_x);
6937 
6938   movq(op1, Address(x, len, Address::times_4,  0));
6939   rorq(op1, 32);
6940 
6941   bind(L_multiply);
6942   subl(zlen, 2);
6943   movq(sum, Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4,  0));
6944 
6945   // Multiply 64 bit by 64 bit and add 64 bits lower half and upper 64 bits as carry.
6946   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6947     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, tmp2);
6948   }
6949   else {
6950     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
6951   }
6952 
6953   movq(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4, 0), sum);
6954 
6955   jmp(L_third_loop);
6956   bind(L_third_loop_exit);
6957 
6958   // Fourth loop
6959   // Add 64 bit long carry into z with carry propogation.
6960   // Uses offsetted zlen.
6961   add_one_64(z, zlen, carry, tmp1);
6962 
6963   pop(len);
6964   pop(zlen);
6965   jmp(L_second_loop);
6966 
6967   // Next infrequent code is moved outside loops.
6968   bind(L_last_x);
6969   movl(op1, Address(x, 0));
6970   jmp(L_multiply);
6971 
6972   bind(L_second_loop_exit);
6973   pop(len);
6974   pop(zlen);
6975   pop(len);
6976   pop(zlen);
6977 
6978   // Fifth loop
6979   // Shift z left 1 bit.
6980   lshift_by_1(x, len, z, zlen, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, tmp4);
6981 
6982   // z[zlen-1] |= x[len-1] & 1;
6983   movl(tmp3, Address(x, len, Address::times_4, -4));
6984   andl(tmp3, 1);
6985   orl(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4,  -4), tmp3);
6986 
6987   pop(tmp5);
6988   pop(tmp4);
6989   pop(tmp3);
6990   pop(tmp2);
6991   pop(tmp1);
6992 }
6993 
6994 /**
6995  * Helper function for mul_add()
6996  * Multiply the in[] by int k and add to out[] starting at offset offs using
6997  * 128 bit by 32 bit multiply and return the carry in tmp5.
6998  * Only quad int aligned length of in[] is operated on in this function.
6999  * k is in rdxReg for BMI2Instructions, for others it is in tmp2.
7000  * This function preserves out, in and k registers.
7001  * len and offset point to the appropriate index in "in" & "out" correspondingly
7002  * tmp5 has the carry.
7003  * other registers are temporary and are modified.
7004  *
7005  */
7006 void MacroAssembler::mul_add_128_x_32_loop(Register out, Register in,
7007   Register offset, Register len, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7008   Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
7009 
7010   Label L_first_loop, L_first_loop_exit;
7011 
7012   movl(tmp1, len);
7013   shrl(tmp1, 2);
7014 
7015   bind(L_first_loop);
7016   subl(tmp1, 1);
7017   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_first_loop_exit);
7018 
7019   subl(len, 4);
7020   subl(offset, 4);
7021 
7022   Register op2 = tmp2;
7023   const Register sum = tmp3;
7024   const Register op1 = tmp4;
7025   const Register carry = tmp5;
7026 
7027   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7028     op2 = rdxReg;
7029   }
7030 
7031   movq(op1, Address(in, len, Address::times_4,  8));
7032   rorq(op1, 32);
7033   movq(sum, Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  8));
7034   rorq(sum, 32);
7035   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7036     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, raxReg);
7037   }
7038   else {
7039     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
7040   }
7041   // Store back in big endian from little endian
7042   rorq(sum, 0x20);
7043   movq(Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  8), sum);
7044 
7045   movq(op1, Address(in, len, Address::times_4,  0));
7046   rorq(op1, 32);
7047   movq(sum, Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  0));
7048   rorq(sum, 32);
7049   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7050     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, raxReg);
7051   }
7052   else {
7053     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
7054   }
7055   // Store back in big endian from little endian
7056   rorq(sum, 0x20);
7057   movq(Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  0), sum);
7058 
7059   jmp(L_first_loop);
7060   bind(L_first_loop_exit);
7061 }
7062 
7063 /**
7064  * Code for BigInteger::mulAdd() intrinsic
7065  *
7066  * rdi: out
7067  * rsi: in
7068  * r11: offs (out.length - offset)
7069  * rcx: len
7070  * r8:  k
7071  * r12: tmp1
7072  * r13: tmp2
7073  * r14: tmp3
7074  * r15: tmp4
7075  * rbx: tmp5
7076  * Multiply the in[] by word k and add to out[], return the carry in rax
7077  */
7078 void MacroAssembler::mul_add(Register out, Register in, Register offs,
7079    Register len, Register k, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7080    Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
7081 
7082   Label L_carry, L_last_in, L_done;
7083 
7084 // carry = 0;
7085 // for (int j=len-1; j >= 0; j--) {
7086 //    long product = (in[j] & LONG_MASK) * kLong +
7087 //                   (out[offs] & LONG_MASK) + carry;
7088 //    out[offs--] = (int)product;
7089 //    carry = product >>> 32;
7090 // }
7091 //
7092   push(tmp1);
7093   push(tmp2);
7094   push(tmp3);
7095   push(tmp4);
7096   push(tmp5);
7097 
7098   Register op2 = tmp2;
7099   const Register sum = tmp3;
7100   const Register op1 = tmp4;
7101   const Register carry =  tmp5;
7102 
7103   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7104     op2 = rdxReg;
7105     movl(op2, k);
7106   }
7107   else {
7108     movl(op2, k);
7109   }
7110 
7111   xorq(carry, carry);
7112 
7113   //First loop
7114 
7115   //Multiply in[] by k in a 4 way unrolled loop using 128 bit by 32 bit multiply
7116   //The carry is in tmp5
7117   mul_add_128_x_32_loop(out, in, offs, len, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, tmp4, tmp5, rdxReg, raxReg);
7118 
7119   //Multiply the trailing in[] entry using 64 bit by 32 bit, if any
7120   decrementl(len);
7121   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_carry);
7122   decrementl(len);
7123   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_last_in);
7124 
7125   movq(op1, Address(in, len, Address::times_4,  0));
7126   rorq(op1, 32);
7127 
7128   subl(offs, 2);
7129   movq(sum, Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  0));
7130   rorq(sum, 32);
7131 
7132   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7133     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, raxReg);
7134   }
7135   else {
7136     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
7137   }
7138 
7139   // Store back in big endian from little endian
7140   rorq(sum, 0x20);
7141   movq(Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  0), sum);
7142 
7143   testl(len, len);
7144   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_carry);
7145 
7146   //Multiply the last in[] entry, if any
7147   bind(L_last_in);
7148   movl(op1, Address(in, 0));
7149   movl(sum, Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  -4));
7150 
7151   movl(raxReg, k);
7152   mull(op1); //tmp4 * eax -> edx:eax
7153   addl(sum, carry);
7154   adcl(rdxReg, 0);
7155   addl(sum, raxReg);
7156   adcl(rdxReg, 0);
7157   movl(carry, rdxReg);
7158 
7159   movl(Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  -4), sum);
7160 
7161   bind(L_carry);
7162   //return tmp5/carry as carry in rax
7163   movl(rax, carry);
7164 
7165   bind(L_done);
7166   pop(tmp5);
7167   pop(tmp4);
7168   pop(tmp3);
7169   pop(tmp2);
7170   pop(tmp1);
7171 }
7172 #endif
7173 
7174 /**
7175  * Emits code to update CRC-32 with a byte value according to constants in table
7176  *
7177  * @param [in,out]crc   Register containing the crc.
7178  * @param [in]val       Register containing the byte to fold into the CRC.
7179  * @param [in]table     Register containing the table of crc constants.
7180  *
7181  * uint32_t crc;
7182  * val = crc_table[(val ^ crc) & 0xFF];
7183  * crc = val ^ (crc >> 8);
7184  *
7185  */
7186 void MacroAssembler::update_byte_crc32(Register crc, Register val, Register table) {
7187   xorl(val, crc);
7188   andl(val, 0xFF);
7189   shrl(crc, 8); // unsigned shift
7190   xorl(crc, Address(table, val, Address::times_4, 0));
7191 }
7192 
7193 /**
7194 * Fold four 128-bit data chunks
7195 */
7196 void MacroAssembler::fold_128bit_crc32_avx512(XMMRegister xcrc, XMMRegister xK, XMMRegister xtmp, Register buf, int offset) {
7197   evpclmulhdq(xtmp, xK, xcrc, Assembler::AVX_512bit); // [123:64]
7198   evpclmulldq(xcrc, xK, xcrc, Assembler::AVX_512bit); // [63:0]
7199   evpxorq(xcrc, xcrc, Address(buf, offset), Assembler::AVX_512bit /* vector_len */);
7200   evpxorq(xcrc, xcrc, xtmp, Assembler::AVX_512bit /* vector_len */);
7201 }
7202 
7203 /**
7204  * Fold 128-bit data chunk
7205  */
7206 void MacroAssembler::fold_128bit_crc32(XMMRegister xcrc, XMMRegister xK, XMMRegister xtmp, Register buf, int offset) {
7207   if (UseAVX > 0) {
7208     vpclmulhdq(xtmp, xK, xcrc); // [123:64]
7209     vpclmulldq(xcrc, xK, xcrc); // [63:0]
7210     vpxor(xcrc, xcrc, Address(buf, offset), 0 /* vector_len */);
7211     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7212   } else {
7213     movdqa(xtmp, xcrc);
7214     pclmulhdq(xtmp, xK);   // [123:64]
7215     pclmulldq(xcrc, xK);   // [63:0]
7216     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7217     movdqu(xtmp, Address(buf, offset));
7218     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7219   }
7220 }
7221 
7222 void MacroAssembler::fold_128bit_crc32(XMMRegister xcrc, XMMRegister xK, XMMRegister xtmp, XMMRegister xbuf) {
7223   if (UseAVX > 0) {
7224     vpclmulhdq(xtmp, xK, xcrc);
7225     vpclmulldq(xcrc, xK, xcrc);
7226     pxor(xcrc, xbuf);
7227     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7228   } else {
7229     movdqa(xtmp, xcrc);
7230     pclmulhdq(xtmp, xK);
7231     pclmulldq(xcrc, xK);
7232     pxor(xcrc, xbuf);
7233     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7234   }
7235 }
7236 
7237 /**
7238  * 8-bit folds to compute 32-bit CRC
7239  *
7240  * uint64_t xcrc;
7241  * timesXtoThe32[xcrc & 0xFF] ^ (xcrc >> 8);
7242  */
7243 void MacroAssembler::fold_8bit_crc32(XMMRegister xcrc, Register table, XMMRegister xtmp, Register tmp) {
7244   movdl(tmp, xcrc);
7245   andl(tmp, 0xFF);
7246   movdl(xtmp, Address(table, tmp, Address::times_4, 0));
7247   psrldq(xcrc, 1); // unsigned shift one byte
7248   pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7249 }
7250 
7251 /**
7252  * uint32_t crc;
7253  * timesXtoThe32[crc & 0xFF] ^ (crc >> 8);
7254  */
7255 void MacroAssembler::fold_8bit_crc32(Register crc, Register table, Register tmp) {
7256   movl(tmp, crc);
7257   andl(tmp, 0xFF);
7258   shrl(crc, 8);
7259   xorl(crc, Address(table, tmp, Address::times_4, 0));
7260 }
7261 
7262 /**
7263  * @param crc   register containing existing CRC (32-bit)
7264  * @param buf   register pointing to input byte buffer (byte*)
7265  * @param len   register containing number of bytes
7266  * @param table register that will contain address of CRC table
7267  * @param tmp   scratch register
7268  */
7269 void MacroAssembler::kernel_crc32(Register crc, Register buf, Register len, Register table, Register tmp) {
7270   assert_different_registers(crc, buf, len, table, tmp, rax);
7271 
7272   Label L_tail, L_tail_restore, L_tail_loop, L_exit, L_align_loop, L_aligned;
7273   Label L_fold_tail, L_fold_128b, L_fold_512b, L_fold_512b_loop, L_fold_tail_loop;
7274 
7275   // For EVEX with VL and BW, provide a standard mask, VL = 128 will guide the merge
7276   // context for the registers used, where all instructions below are using 128-bit mode
7277   // On EVEX without VL and BW, these instructions will all be AVX.
7278   lea(table, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
7279   notl(crc); // ~crc
7280   cmpl(len, 16);
7281   jcc(Assembler::less, L_tail);
7282 
7283   // Align buffer to 16 bytes
7284   movl(tmp, buf);
7285   andl(tmp, 0xF);
7286   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_aligned);
7287   subl(tmp,  16);
7288   addl(len, tmp);
7289 
7290   align(4);
7291   BIND(L_align_loop);
7292   movsbl(rax, Address(buf, 0)); // load byte with sign extension
7293   update_byte_crc32(crc, rax, table);
7294   increment(buf);
7295   incrementl(tmp);
7296   jccb(Assembler::less, L_align_loop);
7297 
7298   BIND(L_aligned);
7299   movl(tmp, len); // save
7300   shrl(len, 4);
7301   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_tail_restore);
7302 
7303   // Fold crc into first bytes of vector
7304   movdqa(xmm1, Address(buf, 0));
7305   movdl(rax, xmm1);
7306   xorl(crc, rax);
7307   if (VM_Version::supports_sse4_1()) {
7308     pinsrd(xmm1, crc, 0);
7309   } else {
7310     pinsrw(xmm1, crc, 0);
7311     shrl(crc, 16);
7312     pinsrw(xmm1, crc, 1);
7313   }
7314   addptr(buf, 16);
7315   subl(len, 4); // len > 0
7316   jcc(Assembler::less, L_fold_tail);
7317 
7318   movdqa(xmm2, Address(buf,  0));
7319   movdqa(xmm3, Address(buf, 16));
7320   movdqa(xmm4, Address(buf, 32));
7321   addptr(buf, 48);
7322   subl(len, 3);
7323   jcc(Assembler::lessEqual, L_fold_512b);
7324 
7325   // Fold total 512 bits of polynomial on each iteration,
7326   // 128 bits per each of 4 parallel streams.
7327   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr() + 32));
7328 
7329   align(32);
7330   BIND(L_fold_512b_loop);
