7331   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, buf,  0);
7332   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm2, xmm0, xmm5, buf, 16);
7333   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm3, xmm0, xmm5, buf, 32);
7334   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm4, xmm0, xmm5, buf, 48);
7335   addptr(buf, 64);
7336   subl(len, 4);
7337   jcc(Assembler::greater, L_fold_512b_loop);
7338 
7339   // Fold 512 bits to 128 bits.
7340   BIND(L_fold_512b);
7341   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr() + 16));
7342   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, xmm2);
7343   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, xmm3);
7344   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, xmm4);
7345 
7346   // Fold the rest of 128 bits data chunks
7347   BIND(L_fold_tail);
7348   addl(len, 3);
7349   jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_fold_128b);
7350   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr() + 16));
7351 
7352   BIND(L_fold_tail_loop);
7353   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, buf,  0);
7354   addptr(buf, 16);
7355   decrementl(len);
7356   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_fold_tail_loop);
7357 
7358   // Fold 128 bits in xmm1 down into 32 bits in crc register.
7359   BIND(L_fold_128b);
7360   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr()));
7361   if (UseAVX > 0) {
7362     vpclmulqdq(xmm2, xmm0, xmm1, 0x1);
7363     vpand(xmm3, xmm0, xmm2, 0 /* vector_len */);
7364     vpclmulqdq(xmm0, xmm0, xmm3, 0x1);
7365   } else {
7366     movdqa(xmm2, xmm0);
7367     pclmulqdq(xmm2, xmm1, 0x1);
7368     movdqa(xmm3, xmm0);
7369     pand(xmm3, xmm2);
7370     pclmulqdq(xmm0, xmm3, 0x1);
7371   }
7372   psrldq(xmm1, 8);
7373   psrldq(xmm2, 4);
7374   pxor(xmm0, xmm1);
7375   pxor(xmm0, xmm2);
7376 
7377   // 8 8-bit folds to compute 32-bit CRC.
7378   for (int j = 0; j < 4; j++) {
7379     fold_8bit_crc32(xmm0, table, xmm1, rax);
7380   }
7381   movdl(crc, xmm0); // mov 32 bits to general register
7382   for (int j = 0; j < 4; j++) {
7383     fold_8bit_crc32(crc, table, rax);
7384   }
7385 
7386   BIND(L_tail_restore);
7387   movl(len, tmp); // restore
7388   BIND(L_tail);
7389   andl(len, 0xf);
7390   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
7391 
7392   // Fold the rest of bytes
7393   align(4);
7394   BIND(L_tail_loop);
7395   movsbl(rax, Address(buf, 0)); // load byte with sign extension
7396   update_byte_crc32(crc, rax, table);
7397   increment(buf);
7398   decrementl(len);
7399   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_tail_loop);
7400 
7401   BIND(L_exit);
7402   notl(crc); // ~c
7403 }
7404 
7405 #ifdef _LP64
7406 // S. Gueron / Information Processing Letters 112 (2012) 184
7407 // Algorithm 4: Computing carry-less multiplication using a precomputed lookup table.
7408 // Input: A 32 bit value B = [byte3, byte2, byte1, byte0].
7409 // Output: the 64-bit carry-less product of B * CONST
7410 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg4(Register in, uint32_t n,
7411                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3) {
7412   lea(tmp3, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::crc32c_table_addr()));
7413   if (n > 0) {
7414     addq(tmp3, n * 256 * 8);
7415   }
7416   //    Q1 = TABLEExt[n][B & 0xFF];
7417   movl(tmp1, in);
7418   andl(tmp1, 0x000000FF);
7419   shll(tmp1, 3);
7420   addq(tmp1, tmp3);
7421   movq(tmp1, Address(tmp1, 0));
7422 
7423   //    Q2 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 8 & 0xFF];
7424   movl(tmp2, in);
7425   shrl(tmp2, 8);
7426   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7427   shll(tmp2, 3);
7428   addq(tmp2, tmp3);
7429   movq(tmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7430 
7431   shlq(tmp2, 8);
7432   xorq(tmp1, tmp2);
7433 
7434   //    Q3 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 16 & 0xFF];
7435   movl(tmp2, in);
7436   shrl(tmp2, 16);
7437   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7438   shll(tmp2, 3);
7439   addq(tmp2, tmp3);
7440   movq(tmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7441 
7442   shlq(tmp2, 16);
7443   xorq(tmp1, tmp2);
7444 
7445   //    Q4 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 24 & 0xFF];
7446   shrl(in, 24);
7447   andl(in, 0x000000FF);
7448   shll(in, 3);
7449   addq(in, tmp3);
7450   movq(in, Address(in, 0));
7451 
7452   shlq(in, 24);
7453   xorq(in, tmp1);
7454   //    return Q1 ^ Q2 << 8 ^ Q3 << 16 ^ Q4 << 24;
7455 }
7456 
7457 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_pclmulqdq(XMMRegister w_xtmp1,
7458                                       Register in_out,
7459                                       uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7460                                       XMMRegister w_xtmp2,
7461                                       Register tmp1,
7462                                       Register n_tmp2, Register n_tmp3) {
7463   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7464     movdl(w_xtmp1, in_out); // modified blindly
7465 
7466     movl(tmp1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index);
7467     movdl(w_xtmp2, tmp1);
7468     pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, 0);
7469 
7470     movdq(in_out, w_xtmp1);
7471   } else {
7472     crc32c_ipl_alg4(in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index, tmp1, n_tmp2, n_tmp3);
7473   }
7474 }
7475 
7476 // Recombination Alternative 2: No bit-reflections
7477 // T1 = (CRC_A * U1) << 1
7478 // T2 = (CRC_B * U2) << 1
7479 // C1 = T1 >> 32
7480 // C2 = T2 >> 32
7481 // T1 = T1 & 0xFFFFFFFF
7482 // T2 = T2 & 0xFFFFFFFF
7483 // T1 = CRC32(0, T1)
7484 // T2 = CRC32(0, T2)
7485 // C1 = C1 ^ T1
7486 // C2 = C2 ^ T2
7487 // CRC = C1 ^ C2 ^ CRC_C
7488 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_rec_alt2(uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported, Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7489                                      XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7490                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2,
7491                                      Register n_tmp3) {
7492   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7493   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp2, in1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7494   shlq(in_out, 1);
7495   movl(tmp1, in_out);
7496   shrq(in_out, 32);
7497   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7498   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7499   xorl(in_out, tmp2); // we don't care about upper 32 bit contents here
7500   shlq(in1, 1);
7501   movl(tmp1, in1);
7502   shrq(in1, 32);
7503   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7504   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7505   xorl(in1, tmp2);
7506   xorl(in_out, in1);
7507   xorl(in_out, in2);
7508 }
7509 
7510 // Set N to predefined value
7511 // Subtract from a lenght of a buffer
7512 // execute in a loop:
7513 // CRC_A = 0xFFFFFFFF, CRC_B = 0, CRC_C = 0
7514 // for i = 1 to N do
7515 //  CRC_A = CRC32(CRC_A, A[i])
7516 //  CRC_B = CRC32(CRC_B, B[i])
7517 //  CRC_C = CRC32(CRC_C, C[i])
7518 // end for
7519 // Recombine
7520 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_proc_chunk(uint32_t size, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7521                                        Register in_out1, Register in_out2, Register in_out3,
7522                                        Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7523                                        XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7524                                        Register tmp4, Register tmp5,
7525                                        Register n_tmp6) {
7526   Label L_processPartitions;
7527   Label L_processPartition;
7528   Label L_exit;
7529 
7530   bind(L_processPartitions);
7531   cmpl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7532   jcc(Assembler::less, L_exit);
7533     xorl(tmp1, tmp1);
7534     xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7535     movq(tmp3, in_out2);
7536     addq(tmp3, size);
7537 
7538     bind(L_processPartition);
7539       crc32(in_out3, Address(in_out2, 0), 8);
7540       crc32(tmp1, Address(in_out2, size), 8);
7541       crc32(tmp2, Address(in_out2, size * 2), 8);
7542       addq(in_out2, 8);
7543       cmpq(in_out2, tmp3);
7544       jcc(Assembler::less, L_processPartition);
7545     crc32c_rec_alt2(const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, in_out3, tmp1, tmp2,
7546             w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7547             tmp4, tmp5,
7548             n_tmp6);
7549     addq(in_out2, 2 * size);
7550     subl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7551     jmp(L_processPartitions);
7552 
7553   bind(L_exit);
7554 }
7555 #else
7556 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg4(Register in_out, uint32_t n,
7557                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7558                                      XMMRegister xtmp1, XMMRegister xtmp2) {
7559   lea(tmp3, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::crc32c_table_addr()));
7560   if (n > 0) {
7561     addl(tmp3, n * 256 * 8);
7562   }
7563   //    Q1 = TABLEExt[n][B & 0xFF];
7564   movl(tmp1, in_out);
7565   andl(tmp1, 0x000000FF);
7566   shll(tmp1, 3);
7567   addl(tmp1, tmp3);
7568   movq(xtmp1, Address(tmp1, 0));
7569 
7570   //    Q2 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 8 & 0xFF];
7571   movl(tmp2, in_out);
7572   shrl(tmp2, 8);
7573   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7574   shll(tmp2, 3);
7575   addl(tmp2, tmp3);
7576   movq(xtmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7577 
7578   psllq(xtmp2, 8);
7579   pxor(xtmp1, xtmp2);
7580 
7581   //    Q3 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 16 & 0xFF];
7582   movl(tmp2, in_out);
7583   shrl(tmp2, 16);
7584   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7585   shll(tmp2, 3);
7586   addl(tmp2, tmp3);
7587   movq(xtmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7588 
7589   psllq(xtmp2, 16);
7590   pxor(xtmp1, xtmp2);
7591 
7592   //    Q4 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 24 & 0xFF];
7593   shrl(in_out, 24);
7594   andl(in_out, 0x000000FF);
7595   shll(in_out, 3);
7596   addl(in_out, tmp3);
7597   movq(xtmp2, Address(in_out, 0));
7598 
7599   psllq(xtmp2, 24);
7600   pxor(xtmp1, xtmp2); // Result in CXMM
7601   //    return Q1 ^ Q2 << 8 ^ Q3 << 16 ^ Q4 << 24;
7602 }
7603 
7604 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_pclmulqdq(XMMRegister w_xtmp1,
7605                                       Register in_out,
7606                                       uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7607                                       XMMRegister w_xtmp2,
7608                                       Register tmp1,
7609                                       Register n_tmp2, Register n_tmp3) {
7610   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7611     movdl(w_xtmp1, in_out);
7612 
7613     movl(tmp1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index);
7614     movdl(w_xtmp2, tmp1);
7615     pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, 0);
7616     // Keep result in XMM since GPR is 32 bit in length
7617   } else {
7618     crc32c_ipl_alg4(in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index, tmp1, n_tmp2, n_tmp3, w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2);
7619   }
7620 }
7621 
7622 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_rec_alt2(uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported, Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7623                                      XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7624                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2,
7625                                      Register n_tmp3) {
7626   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7627   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp2, in1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7628 
7629   psllq(w_xtmp1, 1);
7630   movdl(tmp1, w_xtmp1);
7631   psrlq(w_xtmp1, 32);
7632   movdl(in_out, w_xtmp1);
7633 
7634   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7635   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7636   xorl(in_out, tmp2);
7637 
7638   psllq(w_xtmp2, 1);
7639   movdl(tmp1, w_xtmp2);
7640   psrlq(w_xtmp2, 32);
7641   movdl(in1, w_xtmp2);
7642 
7643   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7644   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7645   xorl(in1, tmp2);
7646   xorl(in_out, in1);
7647   xorl(in_out, in2);
7648 }
7649 
7650 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_proc_chunk(uint32_t size, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7651                                        Register in_out1, Register in_out2, Register in_out3,
7652                                        Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7653                                        XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7654                                        Register tmp4, Register tmp5,
7655                                        Register n_tmp6) {
7656   Label L_processPartitions;
7657   Label L_processPartition;
7658   Label L_exit;
7659 
7660   bind(L_processPartitions);
7661   cmpl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7662   jcc(Assembler::less, L_exit);
7663     xorl(tmp1, tmp1);
7664     xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7665     movl(tmp3, in_out2);
7666     addl(tmp3, size);
7667 
7668     bind(L_processPartition);
7669       crc32(in_out3, Address(in_out2, 0), 4);
7670       crc32(tmp1, Address(in_out2, size), 4);
7671       crc32(tmp2, Address(in_out2, size*2), 4);
7672       crc32(in_out3, Address(in_out2, 0+4), 4);
7673       crc32(tmp1, Address(in_out2, size+4), 4);
7674       crc32(tmp2, Address(in_out2, size*2+4), 4);
7675       addl(in_out2, 8);
7676       cmpl(in_out2, tmp3);
7677       jcc(Assembler::less, L_processPartition);
7678 
7679         push(tmp3);
7680         push(in_out1);
7681         push(in_out2);
7682         tmp4 = tmp3;
7683         tmp5 = in_out1;
7684         n_tmp6 = in_out2;
7685 
7686       crc32c_rec_alt2(const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, in_out3, tmp1, tmp2,
7687             w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7688             tmp4, tmp5,
7689             n_tmp6);
7690 
7691         pop(in_out2);
7692         pop(in_out1);
7693         pop(tmp3);
7694 
7695     addl(in_out2, 2 * size);
7696     subl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7697     jmp(L_processPartitions);
7698 
7699   bind(L_exit);
7700 }
7701 #endif //LP64
7702 
7703 #ifdef _LP64
7704 // Algorithm 2: Pipelined usage of the CRC32 instruction.
7705 // Input: A buffer I of L bytes.
7706 // Output: the CRC32C value of the buffer.
7707 // Notations:
7708 // Write L = 24N + r, with N = floor (L/24).
7709 // r = L mod 24 (0 <= r < 24).
7710 // Consider I as the concatenation of A|B|C|R, where A, B, C, each,
7711 // N quadwords, and R consists of r bytes.
7712 // A[j] = I [8j+7:8j], j= 0, 1, ..., N-1
7713 // B[j] = I [N + 8j+7:N + 8j], j= 0, 1, ..., N-1
7714 // C[j] = I [2N + 8j+7:2N + 8j], j= 0, 1, ..., N-1
7715 // if r > 0 R[j] = I [3N +j], j= 0, 1, ...,r-1
7716 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg2_alt2(Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7717                                           Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7718                                           Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register tmp6,
7719                                           XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7720                                           bool is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7721   uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index[CRC32C_NUM_PRECOMPUTED_CONSTANTS];
7722   Label L_wordByWord;
7723   Label L_byteByByteProlog;
7724   Label L_byteByByte;
7725   Label L_exit;
7726 
7727   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported ) {
7728     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = *(uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr;
7729     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr+1);
7730 
7731     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 2);
7732     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 3);
7733 
7734     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 4);
7735     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 5);
7736     assert((CRC32C_NUM_PRECOMPUTED_CONSTANTS - 1 ) == 5, "Checking whether you declared all of the constants based on the number of \"chunks\"");
7737   } else {
7738     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = 1;
7739     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = 0;
7740 
7741     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = 3;
7742     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = 2;
7743 
7744     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = 5;
7745     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = 4;
7746    }
7747   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_HIGH, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7748                     in2, in1, in_out,
7749                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7750                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7751                     tmp4, tmp5,
7752                     tmp6);
7753   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_MIDDLE, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7754                     in2, in1, in_out,
7755                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7756                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7757                     tmp4, tmp5,
7758                     tmp6);
7759   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_LOW, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7760                     in2, in1, in_out,
7761                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7762                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7763                     tmp4, tmp5,
7764                     tmp6);
7765   movl(tmp1, in2);
7766   andl(tmp1, 0x00000007);
7767   negl(tmp1);
7768   addl(tmp1, in2);
7769   addq(tmp1, in1);
7770 
7771   BIND(L_wordByWord);
7772   cmpq(in1, tmp1);
7773   jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_byteByByteProlog);
7774     crc32(in_out, Address(in1, 0), 4);
7775     addq(in1, 4);
7776     jmp(L_wordByWord);
7777 
7778   BIND(L_byteByByteProlog);
7779   andl(in2, 0x00000007);
7780   movl(tmp2, 1);
7781 
7782   BIND(L_byteByByte);
7783   cmpl(tmp2, in2);
7784   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_exit);
7785     crc32(in_out, Address(in1, 0), 1);
7786     incq(in1);
7787     incl(tmp2);
7788     jmp(L_byteByByte);
7789 
7790   BIND(L_exit);
7791 }
7792 #else
7793 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg2_alt2(Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7794                                           Register tmp1, Register  tmp2, Register tmp3,
7795                                           Register tmp4, Register  tmp5, Register tmp6,
7796                                           XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7797                                           bool is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7798   uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index[CRC32C_NUM_PRECOMPUTED_CONSTANTS];
7799   Label L_wordByWord;
7800   Label L_byteByByteProlog;
7801   Label L_byteByByte;
7802   Label L_exit;
7803 
7804   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7805     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = *(uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr;
7806     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 1);
7807 
7808     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 2);
7809     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 3);
7810 
7811     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 4);
7812     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 5);
7813   } else {
7814     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = 1;
7815     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = 0;
7816 
7817     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = 3;
7818     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = 2;
7819 
7820     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = 5;
7821     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = 4;
7822   }
7823   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_HIGH, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7824                     in2, in1, in_out,
7825                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7826                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7827                     tmp4, tmp5,
7828                     tmp6);
7829   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_MIDDLE, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7830                     in2, in1, in_out,
7831                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7832                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7833                     tmp4, tmp5,
7834                     tmp6);
7835   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_LOW, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7836                     in2, in1, in_out,
7837                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7838                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7839                     tmp4, tmp5,
7840                     tmp6);
7841   movl(tmp1, in2);
7842   andl(tmp1, 0x00000007);
7843   negl(tmp1);
7844   addl(tmp1, in2);
7845   addl(tmp1, in1);
7846 
7847   BIND(L_wordByWord);
7848   cmpl(in1, tmp1);
7849   jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_byteByByteProlog);
7850     crc32(in_out, Address(in1,0), 4);
7851     addl(in1, 4);
7852     jmp(L_wordByWord);
7853 
7854   BIND(L_byteByByteProlog);
7855   andl(in2, 0x00000007);
7856   movl(tmp2, 1);
7857 
7858   BIND(L_byteByByte);
7859   cmpl(tmp2, in2);
7860   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_exit);
7861     movb(tmp1, Address(in1, 0));
7862     crc32(in_out, tmp1, 1);
7863     incl(in1);
7864     incl(tmp2);
7865     jmp(L_byteByByte);
7866 
7867   BIND(L_exit);
7868 }
7869 #endif // LP64
7870 #undef BIND
7871 #undef BLOCK_COMMENT
7872 
7873 // Compress char[] array to byte[].
7874 //   ..\jdk\src\java.base\share\classes\java\lang\StringUTF16.java
7875 //   @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate
7876 //   private static int compress(char[] src, int srcOff, byte[] dst, int dstOff, int len) {
7877 //     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
7878 //       int c = src[srcOff++];
7879 //       if (c >>> 8 != 0) {
7880 //         return 0;
7881 //       }
7882 //       dst[dstOff++] = (byte)c;
7883 //     }
7884 //     return len;
7885 //   }
7886 void MacroAssembler::char_array_compress(Register src, Register dst, Register len,
7887   XMMRegister tmp1Reg, XMMRegister tmp2Reg,
7888   XMMRegister tmp3Reg, XMMRegister tmp4Reg,
7889   Register tmp5, Register result) {
7890   Label copy_chars_loop, return_length, return_zero, done;
7891 
7892   // rsi: src
7893   // rdi: dst
7894   // rdx: len
7895   // rcx: tmp5
7896   // rax: result
7897 
7898   // rsi holds start addr of source char[] to be compressed
7899   // rdi holds start addr of destination byte[]
7900   // rdx holds length
7901 
7902   assert(len != result, "");
7903 
7904   // save length for return
7905   push(len);
7906 
7907   if ((AVX3Threshold == 0) && (UseAVX > 2) && // AVX512
7908     VM_Version::supports_avx512vlbw() &&
7909     VM_Version::supports_bmi2()) {
7910 
7911     Label copy_32_loop, copy_loop_tail, below_threshold;
7912 
7913     // alignment
7914     Label post_alignment;
7915 
7916     // if length of the string is less than 16, handle it in an old fashioned way
7917     testl(len, -32);
7918     jcc(Assembler::zero, below_threshold);
7919 
7920     // First check whether a character is compressable ( <= 0xFF).
7921     // Create mask to test for Unicode chars inside zmm vector
7922     movl(result, 0x00FF);
7923     evpbroadcastw(tmp2Reg, result, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7924 
7925     testl(len, -64);
7926     jcc(Assembler::zero, post_alignment);
7927 
7928     movl(tmp5, dst);
7929     andl(tmp5, (32 - 1));
7930     negl(tmp5);
7931     andl(tmp5, (32 - 1));
7932 
7933     // bail out when there is nothing to be done
7934     testl(tmp5, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7935     jcc(Assembler::zero, post_alignment);
7936 
7937     // ~(~0 << len), where len is the # of remaining elements to process
7938     movl(result, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7939     shlxl(result, result, tmp5);
7940     notl(result);
7941     kmovdl(k3, result);
7942 
7943     evmovdquw(tmp1Reg, k3, Address(src, 0), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7944     evpcmpuw(k2, k3, tmp1Reg, tmp2Reg, Assembler::le, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7945     ktestd(k2, k3);
7946     jcc(Assembler::carryClear, return_zero);
7947 
7948     evpmovwb(Address(dst, 0), k3, tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7949 
7950     addptr(src, tmp5);
7951     addptr(src, tmp5);
7952     addptr(dst, tmp5);
7953     subl(len, tmp5);
7954 
7955     bind(post_alignment);
7956     // end of alignment
7957 
7958     movl(tmp5, len);
7959     andl(tmp5, (32 - 1));    // tail count (in chars)
7960     andl(len, ~(32 - 1));    // vector count (in chars)
7961     jcc(Assembler::zero, copy_loop_tail);
7962 
7963     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
7964     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1));
7965     negptr(len);
7966 
7967     bind(copy_32_loop);
7968     evmovdquw(tmp1Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7969     evpcmpuw(k2, tmp1Reg, tmp2Reg, Assembler::le, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7970     kortestdl(k2, k2);
7971     jcc(Assembler::carryClear, return_zero);
7972 
7973     // All elements in current processed chunk are valid candidates for
7974     // compression. Write a truncated byte elements to the memory.
7975     evpmovwb(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1), tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7976     addptr(len, 32);
7977     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_32_loop);
7978 
7979     bind(copy_loop_tail);
7980     // bail out when there is nothing to be done
7981     testl(tmp5, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7982     jcc(Assembler::zero, return_length);
7983 
7984     movl(len, tmp5);
7985 
7986     // ~(~0 << len), where len is the # of remaining elements to process
7987     movl(result, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7988     shlxl(result, result, len);
7989     notl(result);
7990 
7991     kmovdl(k3, result);
7992 
7993     evmovdquw(tmp1Reg, k3, Address(src, 0), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7994     evpcmpuw(k2, k3, tmp1Reg, tmp2Reg, Assembler::le, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7995     ktestd(k2, k3);
7996     jcc(Assembler::carryClear, return_zero);
7997 
7998     evpmovwb(Address(dst, 0), k3, tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7999     jmp(return_length);
8000 
8001     bind(below_threshold);
8002   }
8003 
8004   if (UseSSE42Intrinsics) {
8005     Label copy_32_loop, copy_16, copy_tail;
8006 
8007     movl(result, len);
8008 
8009     movl(tmp5, 0xff00ff00);   // create mask to test for Unicode chars in vectors
8010 
8011     // vectored compression
8012     andl(len, 0xfffffff0);    // vector count (in chars)
8013     andl(result, 0x0000000f);    // tail count (in chars)
8014     testl(len, len);
8015     jcc(Assembler::zero, copy_16);
8016 
8017     // compress 16 chars per iter
8018     movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
8019     pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);   // store Unicode mask in tmp1Reg
8020     pxor(tmp4Reg, tmp4Reg);
8021 
8022     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
8023     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1));
8024     negptr(len);
8025 
8026     bind(copy_32_loop);
8027     movdqu(tmp2Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));     // load 1st 8 characters
8028     por(tmp4Reg, tmp2Reg);
8029     movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, 16)); // load next 8 characters
8030     por(tmp4Reg, tmp3Reg);
8031     ptest(tmp4Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in next vector
8032     jcc(Assembler::notZero, return_zero);
8033     packuswb(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg);    // only ASCII chars; compress each to 1 byte
8034     movdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1), tmp2Reg);
8035     addptr(len, 16);
8036     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_32_loop);
8037 
8038     // compress next vector of 8 chars (if any)
8039     bind(copy_16);
8040     movl(len, result);
8041     andl(len, 0xfffffff8);    // vector count (in chars)
8042     andl(result, 0x00000007);    // tail count (in chars)
8043     testl(len, len);
8044     jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8045 
8046     movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
8047     pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);   // store Unicode mask in tmp1Reg
8048     pxor(tmp3Reg, tmp3Reg);
8049 
8050     movdqu(tmp2Reg, Address(src, 0));
8051     ptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in vector
8052     jccb(Assembler::notZero, return_zero);
8053     packuswb(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg);    // only LATIN1 chars; compress each to 1 byte
8054     movq(Address(dst, 0), tmp2Reg);
8055     addptr(src, 16);
8056     addptr(dst, 8);
8057 
8058     bind(copy_tail);
8059     movl(len, result);
8060   }
8061   // compress 1 char per iter
8062   testl(len, len);
8063   jccb(Assembler::zero, return_length);
8064   lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
8065   lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1));
8066   negptr(len);
8067 
8068   bind(copy_chars_loop);
8069   load_unsigned_short(result, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
8070   testl(result, 0xff00);      // check if Unicode char
8071   jccb(Assembler::notZero, return_zero);
8072   movb(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1), result);  // ASCII char; compress to 1 byte
8073   increment(len);
8074   jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_chars_loop);
8075 
8076   // if compression succeeded, return length
8077   bind(return_length);
8078   pop(result);
8079   jmpb(done);
8080 
8081   // if compression failed, return 0
8082   bind(return_zero);
8083   xorl(result, result);
8084   addptr(rsp, wordSize);
8085 
8086   bind(done);
8087 }
8088 
8089 // Inflate byte[] array to char[].
8090 //   ..\jdk\src\java.base\share\classes\java\lang\StringLatin1.java
8091 //   @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate
8092 //   private static void inflate(byte[] src, int srcOff, char[] dst, int dstOff, int len) {
8093 //     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
8094 //       dst[dstOff++] = (char)(src[srcOff++] & 0xff);
8095 //     }
8096 //   }
8097 void MacroAssembler::byte_array_inflate(Register src, Register dst, Register len,
8098   XMMRegister tmp1, Register tmp2) {
8099   Label copy_chars_loop, done, below_threshold, avx3_threshold;
8100   // rsi: src
8101   // rdi: dst
8102   // rdx: len
8103   // rcx: tmp2
8104 
8105   // rsi holds start addr of source byte[] to be inflated
8106   // rdi holds start addr of destination char[]
8107   // rdx holds length
8108   assert_different_registers(src, dst, len, tmp2);
8109   movl(tmp2, len);
8110   if ((UseAVX > 2) && // AVX512
8111     VM_Version::supports_avx512vlbw() &&
8112     VM_Version::supports_bmi2()) {
8113 
8114     Label copy_32_loop, copy_tail;
8115     Register tmp3_aliased = len;
8116 
8117     // if length of the string is less than 16, handle it in an old fashioned way
8118     testl(len, -16);
8119     jcc(Assembler::zero, below_threshold);
8120 
8121     testl(len, -1 * AVX3Threshold);
8122     jcc(Assembler::zero, avx3_threshold);
8123 
8124     // In order to use only one arithmetic operation for the main loop we use
8125     // this pre-calculation
8126     andl(tmp2, (32 - 1)); // tail count (in chars), 32 element wide loop
8127     andl(len, -32);     // vector count
8128     jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8129 
8130     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));
8131     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_2));
8132     negptr(len);
8133 
8134 
8135     // inflate 32 chars per iter
8136     bind(copy_32_loop);
8137     vpmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, len, Address::times_1), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8138     evmovdquw(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp1, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8139     addptr(len, 32);
8140     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_32_loop);
8141 
8142     bind(copy_tail);
8143     // bail out when there is nothing to be done
8144     testl(tmp2, -1); // we don't destroy the contents of tmp2 here
8145     jcc(Assembler::zero, done);
8146 
8147     // ~(~0 << length), where length is the # of remaining elements to process
8148     movl(tmp3_aliased, -1);
8149     shlxl(tmp3_aliased, tmp3_aliased, tmp2);
8150     notl(tmp3_aliased);
8151     kmovdl(k2, tmp3_aliased);
8152     evpmovzxbw(tmp1, k2, Address(src, 0), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8153     evmovdquw(Address(dst, 0), k2, tmp1, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8154 
8155     jmp(done);
8156     bind(avx3_threshold);
8157   }
8158   if (UseSSE42Intrinsics) {
8159     Label copy_16_loop, copy_8_loop, copy_bytes, copy_new_tail, copy_tail;
8160 
8161     if (UseAVX > 1) {
8162       andl(tmp2, (16 - 1));
8163       andl(len, -16);
8164       jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_new_tail);
8165     } else {
8166       andl(tmp2, 0x00000007);   // tail count (in chars)
8167       andl(len, 0xfffffff8);    // vector count (in chars)
8168       jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8169     }
8170 
8171     // vectored inflation
8172     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));
8173     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_2));
8174     negptr(len);
8175 
8176     if (UseAVX > 1) {
8177       bind(copy_16_loop);
8178       vpmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, len, Address::times_1), Assembler::AVX_256bit);
8179       vmovdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp1);
8180       addptr(len, 16);
8181       jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_16_loop);
8182 
8183       bind(below_threshold);
8184       bind(copy_new_tail);
8185       movl(len, tmp2);
8186       andl(tmp2, 0x00000007);
8187       andl(len, 0xFFFFFFF8);
8188       jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8189 
8190       pmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, 0));
8191       movdqu(Address(dst, 0), tmp1);
8192       addptr(src, 8);
8193       addptr(dst, 2 * 8);
8194 
8195       jmp(copy_tail, true);
8196     }
8197 
8198     // inflate 8 chars per iter
8199     bind(copy_8_loop);
8200     pmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));  // unpack to 8 words
8201     movdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp1);
8202     addptr(len, 8);
8203     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_8_loop);
8204 
8205     bind(copy_tail);
8206     movl(len, tmp2);
8207 
8208     cmpl(len, 4);
8209     jccb(Assembler::less, copy_bytes);
8210 
8211     movdl(tmp1, Address(src, 0));  // load 4 byte chars
8212     pmovzxbw(tmp1, tmp1);
8213     movq(Address(dst, 0), tmp1);
8214     subptr(len, 4);
8215     addptr(src, 4);
8216     addptr(dst, 8);
8217 
8218     bind(copy_bytes);
8219   } else {
8220     bind(below_threshold);
8221   }
8222 
8223   testl(len, len);
8224   jccb(Assembler::zero, done);
8225   lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));
8226   lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_2));
8227   negptr(len);
8228 
8229   // inflate 1 char per iter
8230   bind(copy_chars_loop);
8231   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));  // load byte char
8232   movw(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp2);  // inflate byte char to word
8233   increment(len);
8234   jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_chars_loop);
8235 
8236   bind(done);
8237 }
8238 
8239 #ifdef _LP64
8240 void MacroAssembler::convert_f2i(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8241   Label done;
8242   cvttss2sil(dst, src);
8243   // Conversion instructions do not match JLS for overflow, underflow and NaN -> fixup in stub
8244   cmpl(dst, 0x80000000); // float_sign_flip
8245   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8246   subptr(rsp, 8);
8247   movflt(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8248   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::f2i_fixup())));
8249   pop(dst);
8250   bind(done);
8251 }
8252 
8253 void MacroAssembler::convert_d2i(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8254   Label done;
8255   cvttsd2sil(dst, src);
8256   // Conversion instructions do not match JLS for overflow, underflow and NaN -> fixup in stub
8257   cmpl(dst, 0x80000000); // float_sign_flip
8258   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8259   subptr(rsp, 8);
8260   movdbl(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8261   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::d2i_fixup())));
8262   pop(dst);
8263   bind(done);
8264 }
8265 
8266 void MacroAssembler::convert_f2l(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8267   Label done;
8268   cvttss2siq(dst, src);
8269   cmp64(dst, ExternalAddress((address) StubRoutines::x86::double_sign_flip()));
8270   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8271   subptr(rsp, 8);
8272   movflt(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8273   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::f2l_fixup())));
8274   pop(dst);
8275   bind(done);
8276 }
8277 
8278 void MacroAssembler::convert_d2l(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8279   Label done;
8280   cvttsd2siq(dst, src);
8281   cmp64(dst, ExternalAddress((address) StubRoutines::x86::double_sign_flip()));
8282   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8283   subptr(rsp, 8);
8284   movdbl(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8285   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::d2l_fixup())));
8286   pop(dst);
8287   bind(done);
8288 }
8289 
8290 void MacroAssembler::cache_wb(Address line)
8291 {
8292   // 64 bit cpus always support clflush
8293   assert(VM_Version::supports_clflush(), "clflush should be available");
8294   bool optimized = VM_Version::supports_clflushopt();
8295   bool no_evict = VM_Version::supports_clwb();
8296 
8297   // prefer clwb (writeback without evict) otherwise
8298   // prefer clflushopt (potentially parallel writeback with evict)
8299   // otherwise fallback on clflush (serial writeback with evict)
8300 
8301   if (optimized) {
8302     if (no_evict) {
8303       clwb(line);
8304     } else {
8305       clflushopt(line);
8306     }
8307   } else {
8308     // no need for fence when using CLFLUSH
8309     clflush(line);
8310   }
8311 }
8312 
8313 void MacroAssembler::cache_wbsync(bool is_pre)
8314 {
8315   assert(VM_Version::supports_clflush(), "clflush should be available");
8316   bool optimized = VM_Version::supports_clflushopt();
8317   bool no_evict = VM_Version::supports_clwb();
8318 
8319   // pick the correct implementation
8320 
8321   if (!is_pre && (optimized || no_evict)) {
8322     // need an sfence for post flush when using clflushopt or clwb
8323     // otherwise no no need for any synchroniaztion
8324 
8325     sfence();
8326   }
8327 }
8328 #endif // _LP64
8329 
8330 Assembler::Condition MacroAssembler::negate_condition(Assembler::Condition cond) {
8331   switch (cond) {
8332     // Note some conditions are synonyms for others
8333     case Assembler::zero:         return Assembler::notZero;
8334     case Assembler::notZero:      return Assembler::zero;
8335     case Assembler::less:         return Assembler::greaterEqual;
8336     case Assembler::lessEqual:    return Assembler::greater;
8337     case Assembler::greater:      return Assembler::lessEqual;
8338     case Assembler::greaterEqual: return Assembler::less;
8339     case Assembler::below:        return Assembler::aboveEqual;
8340     case Assembler::belowEqual:   return Assembler::above;
8341     case Assembler::above:        return Assembler::belowEqual;
8342     case Assembler::aboveEqual:   return Assembler::below;
8343     case Assembler::overflow:     return Assembler::noOverflow;
8344     case Assembler::noOverflow:   return Assembler::overflow;
8345     case Assembler::negative:     return Assembler::positive;
8346     case Assembler::positive:     return Assembler::negative;
8347     case Assembler::parity:       return Assembler::noParity;
8348     case Assembler::noParity:     return Assembler::parity;
8349   }
8350   ShouldNotReachHere(); return Assembler::overflow;
8351 }
8352 
8353 SkipIfEqual::SkipIfEqual(
8354     MacroAssembler* masm, const bool* flag_addr, bool value) {
8355   _masm = masm;
8356   _masm->cmp8(ExternalAddress((address)flag_addr), value);
8357   _masm->jcc(Assembler::equal, _label);
8358 }
8359 
8360 SkipIfEqual::~SkipIfEqual() {
8361   _masm->bind(_label);
8362 }
8363 
8364 // 32-bit Windows has its own fast-path implementation
8365 // of get_thread
8366 #if !defined(WIN32) || defined(_LP64)
8367 
8368 // This is simply a call to Thread::current()
8369 void MacroAssembler::get_thread(Register thread) {
8370   if (thread != rax) {
8371     push(rax);
8372   }
8373   LP64_ONLY(push(rdi);)
8374   LP64_ONLY(push(rsi);)
8375   push(rdx);
8376   push(rcx);
8377 #ifdef _LP64
8378   push(r8);
8379   push(r9);
8380   push(r10);
8381   push(r11);
8382 #endif
8383 
8384   MacroAssembler::call_VM_leaf_base(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, Thread::current), 0);
8385 
8386 #ifdef _LP64
8387   pop(r11);
8388   pop(r10);
8389   pop(r9);
8390   pop(r8);
8391 #endif
8392   pop(rcx);
8393   pop(rdx);
8394   LP64_ONLY(pop(rsi);)
8395   LP64_ONLY(pop(rdi);)
8396   if (thread != rax) {
8397     mov(thread, rax);
8398     pop(rax);
8399   }
8400 }
8401 
8402 #endif // !WIN32 || _LP64
